    const hideLoader = () => elements.loader.classList.remove('visible');
    
/**
 * [ULTRA-PREMIUM] Affiche une notification avec effets néon, dégradés et animations.
 */
function showToast(message, isError = false, isUndoable = false) {
    const toastId = `toast-${Date.now()}`;
    const toast = document.createElement('div');
    toast.id = toastId;
    
    let duration = isUndoable ? 12000 : 5000;
    
    // --- PALETTES HAUT DE GAMME ---
    // Couleurs selon le type (Succès = Airbus Cyan/Bleu | Erreur = Rose/Rouge vif)
    const gradientIcon = isError ? 'from-rose-500 to-red-600' : 'from-[#00b5e2] to-[#00205b]';
    const shadowGlow = isError ? 'shadow-[0_0_20px_rgba(225,29,72,0.4)]' : 'shadow-[0_0_20px_rgba(0,181,226,0.4)]';
    const iconClass = isError ? 'fa-exclamation text-white' : 'fa-check text-white';
    const titleText = isError ? 'Action Échouée' : 'Action Réussie';
    const titleGradient = isError ? 'from-rose-600 to-red-800' : 'from-[#00b5e2] to-[#00205b]';
    const progressBarColor = isError ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-rose-500 to-red-600' : 'bg-gradient-to-r from-[#00b5e2] to-[#00205b]';
    const borderGlow = isError ? 'border-red-200' : 'border-[#00b5e2]/30';

    // Bouton d'annulation stylisé avec animation de l'icône
    let undoButtonHtml = '';
    if (isUndoable) {
        undoButtonHtml = `
            <button onclick="undoLastChange('${toastId}')" class="ml-4 shrink-0 bg-[#00205b] hover:bg-[#00b5e2] text-white text-[9.5px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest px-3.5 py-2 rounded-xl transition-all shadow-[0_5px_15px_rgba(0,32,91,0.2)] hover:shadow-[0_8px_20px_rgba(0,181,226,0.3)] active:scale-95 flex items-center gap-1.5 group">
                <i class="fas fa-undo-alt group-hover:-rotate-180 transition-transform duration-500"></i> Annuler
            </button>
        `;
    }

    // Le conteneur principal (Glassmorphism intense, hauteur 64px)
    toast.className = `relative overflow-hidden bg-white/90 backdrop-blur-2xl border ${borderGlow} shadow-[0_20px_50px_-10px_rgba(0,32,91,0.15)] rounded-[1.25rem] px-4 flex items-center w-full h-[64px] pointer-events-auto transform transition-all duration-500 translate-x-[120%] opacity-0 group/toast`;
    
    toast.innerHTML = `
        <div class="w-10 h-10 rounded-[0.85rem] bg-gradient-to-br ${gradientIcon} ${shadowGlow} flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 mr-4 transform group-hover/toast:scale-105 transition-transform duration-300">
            <i class="fas ${iconClass} text-lg drop-shadow-md"></i>
        </div>

        <div class="flex-grow min-w-0 flex flex-col justify-center h-full pt-0.5">
            <p class="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest leading-none mb-1.5 bg-clip-text text-transparent bg-gradient-to-r ${titleGradient}">${titleText}</p>
            <p class="text-[11px] font-bold text-gray-500 leading-none whitespace-nowrap">${message}</p>
        </div>

        ${undoButtonHtml}

        <div class="absolute bottom-0 left-0 h-[4px] ${progressBarColor} transition-all duration-100 ease-linear shadow-[0_-2px_10px_rgba(0,0,0,0.1)]" style="width: 100%;" id="progress-${toastId}"></div>

        <div class="absolute -right-10 -top-10 w-32 h-32 bg-white/40 rounded-full blur-2xl pointer-events-none z-[-1]"></div>
    `;

    elements.toastContainer.appendChild(toast);

    // Animation d'entrée fluide
    requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        toast.classList.remove('translate-x-[120%]', 'opacity-0');
        toast.classList.add('translate-x-0', 'opacity-100');
    });

    // Gestion du timer de la barre
    const progressBar = toast.querySelector(`#progress-${toastId}`);
    const startTime = Date.now();
    const progressInterval = setInterval(() => {
        const elapsed = Date.now() - startTime;
        const percentage = Math.max(0, 100 - (elapsed / duration) * 100);
        if (progressBar) progressBar.style.width = `${percentage}%`;
    }, 20);

    // Suppression propre
    const removeToast = () => {
        clearInterval(progressInterval);
        toast.classList.remove('translate-x-0', 'opacity-100');
        toast.classList.add('translate-x-[120%]', 'opacity-0');
        
        setTimeout(() => {
            if (toast.parentElement) toast.remove();
        }, 500);
    };

    setTimeout(removeToast, duration);
}

/**
     * Annule la dernière action (Statut simple, Commentaire ou Mise à jour groupée).
     */
    async function undoLastChange(toastId) {
        // Ferme le toast immédiatement
        const toastElement = document.getElementById(toastId);
        if (toastElement) toastElement.remove();
        
        if (!state.lastAction) return;

        const action = { ...state.lastAction };
        state.lastAction = null; // Empêche de cliquer deux fois

        showLoader(true);
        try {
            if (action.type === 'status') {
                // Annulation d'un clic simple (Matin -> Absent par exemple)
                await setAndSavePresence(action.dateKey, action.oldStatus, action.personnelId);
                showToast(t('toast_mod_canceled'), false);

} else if (action.type === 'details') {
            await serverCall('savePresenceDetails', [action.personnelId, action.dateKey, action.oldComment, action.oldHs]);
            showToast(t('toast_details_restored'), false);

            } else if (action.type === 'mass_update_batch') {
                // [NOUVEAU] Annulation de la modification groupée
                // On envoie tout le paquet de "vieux statuts" au serveur pour restauration
                await serverCall('restorePresencesBatch', [action.oldStatusesBatch]);
                
                await fetchAndRenderTeamView(); // On rafraîchit l'affichage
                showToast(t('toast_mass_cancel'), false);
            }
        } catch (e) {
            showToast(`Erreur lors de l'annulation : ${e.message}`, true);
        } finally {
            hideLoader();
        }
    }

// (Fonction utilitaire pour fermer la modale)
function closeSettingsModal() {
    document.getElementById('settings-modal').classList.add('hidden');
    
    // --- NOUVEAU : Réactiver le scroll de l'arrière-plan ---
    document.body.style.overflow = '';
}

function applyUIPermissions() {
    const isAdmin = state.currentUser?.role === 'Administrateur';
    document.getElementById('add-person-btn').style.display = isAdmin ? 'flex' : 'none';
    document.getElementById('open-settings-btn').style.display = isAdmin ? 'flex' : 'none';
    document.getElementById('mass-update-btn').style.display = isAdmin ? 'flex' : 'none';

    const actionsTab = document.querySelector('[data-tab="actions"]');
    if (actionsTab) actionsTab.style.display = isAdmin ? 'block' : 'none';
    
    // NOUVEAU
    const capaTab = document.querySelector('[data-tab="capa"]');
    if (capaTab) capaTab.style.display = isAdmin ? 'block' : 'none';
}

    /**
 * Initialise la logique du menu déroulant personnalisé pour les postes de travail.
 */
function setupWorkstationDropdown() {
    const button = document.getElementById('workstation-dropdown-button');
    const panel = document.getElementById('workstation-dropdown-panel');
    const buttonText = document.getElementById('workstation-dropdown-text');
    const chevron = button.querySelector('i');
    
    // La liste de vos postes de travail
    const workstations = state.settings.workstations || [];

    // Génère les options avec cases à cocher dans le panneau
    panel.innerHTML = workstations.map(ws => `
        <label class="relative flex cursor-pointer select-none items-center py-2 pl-4 pr-9 text-gray-900 hover:bg-indigo-50 transition-colors">
            <input type="checkbox" name="posteDeTravail" value="${ws}" class="h-4 w-4 rounded border-gray-300 text-indigo-600 focus:ring-indigo-500">
            <span class="ml-3 block truncate font-medium">${ws}</span>
        </label>
    `).join('');

    // Fonction pour mettre à jour le texte du bouton principal
    const updateButtonText = () => {
        const checkedBoxes = panel.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]:checked');
        if (checkedBoxes.length === 0) {
            buttonText.textContent = 'Sélectionner...';
            buttonText.classList.add('text-gray-500');
        } else if (checkedBoxes.length <= 2) {
            buttonText.textContent = Array.from(checkedBoxes).map(cb => cb.value).join(', ');
            buttonText.classList.remove('text-gray-500');
        } else {
            buttonText.textContent = `${checkedBoxes.length} postes sélectionnés`;
            buttonText.classList.remove('text-gray-500');
        }
    };

    // On expose la fonction pour pouvoir l'appeler depuis d'autres endroits
    window.updateWorkstationButtonText = updateButtonText;

    // Gestion des événements
    button.addEventListener('click', () => {
        panel.classList.toggle('hidden');
        chevron.classList.toggle('rotate-180');
    });

    document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        if (!button.contains(e.target) && !panel.contains(e.target) && !panel.classList.contains('hidden')) {
            panel.classList.add('hidden');
            chevron.classList.remove('rotate-180');
        }
    });
    
    panel.addEventListener('change', updateButtonText);
}

/**
 * [FIABILISÉ] Vérifie côté client si l'utilisateur a le droit de modifier une personne.
 * Cette fonction doit refléter la logique de sécurité du backend pour une expérience utilisateur cohérente.
 * @param {object | null} targetPerson L'objet de la personne à modifier.
 * @returns {boolean} Vrai si l'utilisateur peut modifier, sinon faux.
 */
function canUserModify(targetPerson = null) {
    if (!state.currentUser || !targetPerson) return false;

    const userRole = state.currentUser.role;
    const userName = state.currentUser.name;

    // Règle 1: Les administrateurs peuvent tout modifier.
    if (userRole === 'Administrateur') return true;
    
    // Règle 2: Les lecteurs ne peuvent rien modifier.
    if (userRole === 'Lecteur') return false;

    // Règle 3a: Manager (RP, etc.) modifiant un subordonné direct.
    const managerRoles = ['RP', 'Responsable Preparateur', 'Responsable Qualité'];
    if (managerRoles.includes(userRole) && targetPerson.responsableHierarchique === userName) {
        return true;
    }

    // Règle 3b: REAP ou Pilote modifiant un membre de son équipe.
    if (userRole === 'REAP' && targetPerson.chefEquipeAssocie === userName) {
        return true;
    }

    // Règle 3c: Permissions "latérales" (ex: Qualité modifie Qualité).
    const peerPermissions = {
        'Qualité': ['Qualité', 'Responsable Qualité'],
        'Responsable Qualité': ['Qualité', 'Responsable Qualité'],
        'Responsable Preparateur': ['Préparateur', 'Responsable Preparateur'],
        'MFT': ['MFT']
    };
    if (peerPermissions[userRole] && peerPermissions[userRole].includes(targetPerson.role)) {
        return true;
    }

    // Si aucune règle ne correspond, l'action est interdite.
    return false;
}

    /**
 * Initialise la logique pour le défilement horizontal des filtres.
 */
function setupFilterScroller() {
    const container = document.getElementById('filters-scroll-container');
    const leftBtn = document.getElementById('scroll-left-btn');
    const rightBtn = document.getElementById('scroll-right-btn');

    if (!container || !leftBtn || !rightBtn) return;

    const scrollAmount = 250; // Nombre de pixels à défiler par clic

    const updateArrowVisibility = () => {
        const hasOverflow = container.scrollWidth > container.clientWidth;
        
        // S'il n'y a pas de défilement, on cache les deux flèches.
        if (!hasOverflow) {
            leftBtn.classList.add('hidden');
            rightBtn.classList.add('hidden');
            return;
        }

        // Flèche gauche : visible si on n'est pas tout à gauche
        leftBtn.classList.toggle('hidden', container.scrollLeft <= 0);
        
        // Flèche droite : visible si on n'est pas tout à droite
        const maxScrollLeft = container.scrollWidth - container.clientWidth;
        rightBtn.classList.toggle('hidden', container.scrollLeft >= maxScrollLeft - 1);
    };
    
    // Ajout des événements de clic sur les flèches
    leftBtn.onclick = () => container.scrollBy({ left: -scrollAmount, behavior: 'smooth' });
    rightBtn.onclick = () => container.scrollBy({ left: scrollAmount, behavior: 'smooth' });

    // On met à jour la visibilité des flèches à chaque défilement
    container.addEventListener('scroll', updateArrowVisibility);
    
    // On observe les changements de taille pour réévaluer la visibilité
    new ResizeObserver(updateArrowVisibility).observe(container);

    // On vérifie une première fois au cas où le contenu déborderait déjà
    setTimeout(updateArrowVisibility, 50); 
}

function saveFiltersToLocalStorage() {
    try {
        const filtersToSave = {
            roleFilter: state.roleFilter,
            personnelListReapFilter: state.personnelListReapFilter,
            teamViewMonth: elements.monthPicker.value,
            // On sauvegarde les filtres pour chaque mode
            teamViewSelection_production: state.teamViewSelection_production,
            teamViewSelection_support: state.teamViewSelection_support,
        };
        localStorage.setItem('planningAppFilters', JSON.stringify(filtersToSave));
    } catch (e) {
        console.warn("Impossible de sauvegarder les filtres dans localStorage:", e);
    }
}

function loadFiltersFromLocalStorage() {
    try {
        const savedFilters = localStorage.getItem('planningAppFilters');
        if (savedFilters) {
            const filters = JSON.parse(savedFilters);
            state.roleFilter = filters.roleFilter || 'Tous';
            state.personnelListReapFilter = filters.personnelListReapFilter || 'Tous';
            state.teamViewDate = filters.teamViewMonth || new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 7);
            // On charge les filtres pour chaque mode
            state.teamViewSelection_production = filters.teamViewSelection_production || ['Tous'];
            state.teamViewSelection_support = filters.teamViewSelection_support || []; 
        }
    } catch(e) {
        console.warn("Impossible de charger les filtres depuis localStorage:", e);
        // On réinitialise en cas d'erreur
        state.teamViewSelection_production = ['Tous'];
        state.teamViewSelection_support = [];
        localStorage.removeItem('planningAppFilters');
    }
}

function setupTeamFilter() {
    const container = elements.teamViewFilterContainer; 
    if (!container) return;
    container.innerHTML = ''; 

    const createRoleBadge = (role) => {
        if (!role || role === 'Tous') return '';
        let bgColor, textColor, borderClass, text;
        switch (role) {
            case 'REAP': bgColor = 'bg-emerald-50'; textColor = 'text-emerald-700'; borderClass = 'border-emerald-200'; text = 'REAP'; break;
            case 'Pilote': bgColor = 'bg-blue-50'; textColor = 'text-blue-700'; borderClass = 'border-blue-200'; text = 'Pilote'; break;
            case 'RP': bgColor = 'bg-purple-50'; textColor = 'text-purple-700'; borderClass = 'border-purple-200'; text = 'RP'; break;
            case 'Responsable Preparateur': bgColor = 'bg-orange-50'; textColor = 'text-orange-700'; borderClass = 'border-orange-200'; text = 'Resp. Prép.'; break;
            case 'Responsable Qualité': bgColor = 'bg-cyan-50'; textColor = 'text-cyan-700'; borderClass = 'border-cyan-200'; text = 'Resp. Qual.'; break;
            default: return '';
        }
        return `<span class="inline-flex items-center rounded-md px-2 py-0.5 text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest ${bgColor} ${textColor} border ${borderClass} shadow-sm">${t_role(role)}</span>`;
    };

    const optionsWrapper = document.createElement('div');
    optionsWrapper.className = "flex flex-col px-2 pb-16"; 

    const allOptions = [
        { text: 'Tous', value: 'Tous', role: 'Tous' },
        ...state.chefsEquipe.map(manager => ({ 
            text: manager.name, 
            value: `${manager.name} (${manager.role})`,
            role: manager.role 
        }))
    ];

    allOptions.forEach((option) => {
        const optionId = `team-option-${option.value.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, "")}`;
        const isChecked = state.teamViewSelection.includes(option.value);
        
        const label = document.createElement('label');
        label.className = `flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 cursor-pointer rounded-xl transition-all duration-200 mb-1 ${isChecked ? 'bg-[#00b5e2]/10' : 'hover:bg-gray-50'}`;
        label.setAttribute('for', optionId);
        
        const leftGroup = document.createElement('div');
        leftGroup.className = "flex items-center flex-grow overflow-hidden mr-2";

        const checkbox = document.createElement('input');
        checkbox.id = optionId;
        checkbox.value = option.value;
        checkbox.type = 'checkbox';
        checkbox.checked = isChecked;
        checkbox.className = "h-4 w-4 rounded border-gray-300 text-[#00205b] focus:ring-[#00b5e2] cursor-pointer shrink-0";

        const textSpan = document.createElement('span');
        // Remplacement de whitespace-nowrap par break-words leading-tight
        textSpan.className = `ml-3 text-[11px] uppercase tracking-widest break-words leading-tight ${isChecked ? 'font-black text-[#00205b]' : 'font-bold text-gray-600'}`;
        textSpan.textContent = option.role !== 'Tous' ? `${option.text.split('(')[0].trim()} (${t_role(option.role)})` : t('filter_all');
        
        leftGroup.appendChild(checkbox);
        leftGroup.appendChild(textSpan);

        const badgeContainer = document.createElement('div');
        badgeContainer.className = "shrink-0";
        badgeContainer.innerHTML = createRoleBadge(option.role);
        
        label.appendChild(leftGroup);
        if (option.role !== 'Tous') {
            label.appendChild(badgeContainer);
        }
        
        optionsWrapper.appendChild(label);
    });

    const footer = document.createElement('div');
    footer.className = "sticky bottom-0 left-0 w-full bg-white/95 backdrop-blur-md border-t border-gray-100 p-3 z-20 rounded-b-2xl shadow-[0_-10px_15px_rgba(255,255,255,0.9)]"; 
    footer.innerHTML = `<button id="validate-team-filter-btn" class="w-full bg-[#00205b] text-white px-4 h-[42px] rounded-xl text-[11px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest hover:bg-[#00b5e2] transition-all shadow-md">${t('btn_apply')}</button>`;
    
    container.appendChild(optionsWrapper);
    container.appendChild(footer);

    const shiftFilterContainer = document.getElementById('shift-filter-container');
    if (shiftFilterContainer) {
        const selections = state.teamViewSelection;
        const reapSelectionsCount = selections.filter(s => s.includes('(REAP)')).length;
        const shouldShowShiftFilter = reapSelectionsCount === 2 && selections.length === 2;

        if (shouldShowShiftFilter) {
            shiftFilterContainer.classList.remove('hidden');
        } else {
            shiftFilterContainer.classList.add('hidden');
            state.shiftFilter = null; 
            document.querySelectorAll('#shift-filter-buttons button').forEach(btn => {
                const shift = btn.getAttribute('data-shift');
                btn.setAttribute('aria-selected', shift === 'null');
            });
        }
    }

    updateTeamFilterButtonText();
}

function updateTeamFilterButtonText() {
    const selection = state.teamViewSelection; // Contient la valeur complète, ex: "John Doe (REAP)"
    const buttonText = elements.teamViewFilterButtonText;

    if (selection.length === 0 || selection.includes("Tous")) {
        buttonText.textContent = t('filter_all_teams'); // Correction de la clé de traduction ici !
    } else if (selection.length === 1) {
        const selectedValue = selection[0];
        
        // On cherche le manager dans notre liste d'objets pour récupérer son nom "propre"
        const manager = state.chefsEquipe.find(m => `${m.name} (${m.role})` === selectedValue);
        
        if (manager) {
            buttonText.textContent = manager.name; // Affiche "John Doe"
        } else {
            // Fallback au cas où (ex: RP en mode support non trouvé, etc.)
            buttonText.textContent = selectedValue.replace(/ \(.+\)$/, '');
        }
    } else {
        // Utilisation de la traduction pour le pluriel
        buttonText.textContent = `${selection.length} ${t('selected_teams')}`;
    }
}

function renderUserProfile() {
    // Ne fait plus rien

/**
 * Alterne l'affichage entre le personnel actif et archivé
 */
function toggleArchiveView() {
    state.showArchived = !state.showArchived;
    const btn = document.getElementById('toggle-archive-btn');
    const searchInput = document.getElementById('search-personnel');
    
    if (state.showArchived) {
        // Style visuel quand on est dans les archives (Orange/Ambre)
        btn.classList.remove('text-[#00b5e2]', 'bg-white', 'hover:bg-[#00205b]', 'hover:text-white');
        btn.classList.add('text-white', 'bg-amber-500', 'border-amber-600', 'hover:bg-amber-600');
        btn.title = "Voir le personnel actif";
        searchInput.placeholder = "CHERCHER DANS LES ARCHIVES...";
        showToast(t('toast_archive_mode'));
    } else {
        // Style visuel normal (Actifs)
        btn.classList.add('text-[#00b5e2]', 'bg-white', 'hover:bg-[#00205b]', 'hover:text-white');
        btn.classList.remove('text-white', 'bg-amber-500', 'border-amber-600', 'hover:bg-amber-600');
        btn.title = "Voir les archives";
        searchInput.placeholder = "CHERCHER UN NOM...";
        showToast(t('toast_active_mode'));
    }
    
    // On relance le dessin de la liste
    renderPersonnelList();
}

/**
 * [OPTIMISÉ & CORRIGÉ]
 * Affiche et synchronise la liste du personnel avec gestion des ARCHIVES et des FILTRES.
 */
function renderPersonnelList() {
    // 1. Filtrage initial par Statut (Archive ou Actif)
    let filtered = state.personnel.filter(p => {
        if (state.showArchived) {
            return p.statut === 'Archivé';
        } else {
            return p.statut !== 'Archivé';
        }
    });

    // 2. Application des filtres de rôles (Production / Support)
    if (state.roleFilter !== 'Tous') {
        filtered = filtered.filter(p => p.role === state.roleFilter);
    }

    // 3. Application du filtre REAP (CORRIGÉ : s'applique tout le temps)
    if (state.personnelListReapFilter !== 'Tous') {
        filtered = filtered.filter(p => p.chefEquipeAssocie === state.personnelListReapFilter);
    }

    // 4. Application de la recherche textuelle
    const query = state.searchQuery.toLowerCase().trim();
    if (query) {
        filtered = filtered.filter(p => `${p.prenom} ${p.nom}`.toLowerCase().includes(query));
    }
    
    // 5. Logique de tri
    const roleOrder = { 'RP': 1, 'REAP': 2, 'MFT': 3, 'Apprenti': 4, 'Responsable Qualité': 5, 'Qualité': 6, 'Responsable Preparateur': 7, 'Préparateur': 8, 'Compagnon': 9, 'Intérimaire': 10 };
    if (state.personnelSort === 'prenom-asc') {
        filtered.sort((a, b) => a.prenom.localeCompare(b.prenom));
    } else if (state.personnelSort === 'prenom-desc') {
        filtered.sort((a, b) => b.prenom.localeCompare(a.prenom));
    } else if (state.personnelSort === 'role-asc') {
        filtered.sort((a, b) => (roleOrder[a.role] || 99) - (roleOrder[b.role] || 99) || a.prenom.localeCompare(b.prenom));
    }

    // --- Synchronisation avec le DOM ---
    const listElement = elements.personnelList;
    listElement.innerHTML = ''; // On vide pour reconstruire proprement avec les nouveaux boutons

    if (filtered.length === 0) {
        listElement.innerHTML = `<li class="text-center text-gray-500 p-4 bg-gray-50 rounded-xl border border-dashed border-gray-300">
            ${state.showArchived ? 'Aucune archive trouvée.' : 'Aucun personnel trouvé pour ces critères.'}
        </li>`;
        return;
    }

filtered.forEach(person => {
        const li = document.createElement('li');
        li.dataset.personId = person.id;
        const isSelected = state.selectedPersonnelId === person.id;
        
        // 1. Définition des couleurs selon le rôle (Avatar)
        let avatarBg = 'bg-gray-100', avatarText = 'text-gray-600', avatarBorder = 'border-gray-200';
        if (person.role === 'Compagnon') { avatarBg = 'bg-sky-100'; avatarText = 'text-sky-600'; avatarBorder = 'border-sky-200'; }
        else if (person.role === 'Intérimaire') { avatarBg = 'bg-fuchsia-100'; avatarText = 'text-fuchsia-600'; avatarBorder = 'border-fuchsia-200'; }
        else if (person.role === 'RP') { avatarBg = 'bg-purple-100'; avatarText = 'text-purple-700'; avatarBorder = 'border-purple-300'; }
        else if (person.role === 'REAP') { avatarBg = 'bg-emerald-100'; avatarText = 'text-emerald-700'; avatarBorder = 'border-emerald-300'; }
        else if (person.role === 'Pilote') { avatarBg = 'bg-blue-100'; avatarText = 'text-blue-700'; avatarBorder = 'border-blue-300'; }
        
        // Initiales (ex: Adrien Morel -> AM)
        const initials = ((person.prenom ? person.prenom.charAt(0) : '') + (person.nom ? person.nom.charAt(0) : '')).toUpperCase();

        // 2. Style de la carte (Sélectionné vs Normal)
        const liClasses = isSelected 
            ? 'bg-[#00205b] text-white shadow-[0_15px_30px_-5px_rgba(0,32,91,0.4)] border-[#00205b] is-selected z-10' 
            : 'bg-white text-gray-800 border-gray-100 hover:border-[#00b5e2]/40 hover:shadow-lg';
            
        li.className = `personnel-card rounded-2xl border-2 transition-all cursor-pointer flex justify-between items-center group overflow-hidden ${liClasses}`;
        
        const posteInfo = person.posteDeTravail ? person.posteDeTravail : '';
        const sectionInfo = person.section ? `Sec. ${person.section}` : '';
        const combinedInfo = [t_role(person.role), posteInfo, sectionInfo].filter(Boolean).join(' • ');

        // Textes et couleurs
        const nameColor = isSelected ? 'text-white' : 'text-[#00205b] group-hover:text-[#00b5e2]';
        const infoColor = isSelected ? 'text-blue-200' : 'text-gray-400';
        
        // Boutons d'action
        const btnClass = isSelected 
            ? 'text-white/60 hover:text-white hover:bg-white/20' 
            : 'text-gray-300 hover:text-[#00b5e2] hover:bg-[#00b5e2]/10';
        
        let actionBtn = '';
        if (state.showArchived) {
            actionBtn = `<button onclick="reactivatePersonnelHandler('${person.id}'); event.stopPropagation();" class="${btnClass} w-8 h-8 rounded-lg transition-all" title="Remettre en ligne"><i class="fas fa-arrow-up-from-bracket"></i></button>`;
        } else {
            actionBtn = `<button onclick="deletePersonnelHandler('${person.id}'); event.stopPropagation();" class="${isSelected ? 'text-white/60 hover:text-red-400 hover:bg-white/20' : 'text-gray-300 hover:text-red-500 hover:bg-red-50'} w-8 h-8 rounded-lg transition-all" title="Archiver" ${!canUserModify(person) ? 'disabled' : ''}><i class="fas fa-trash-alt"></i></button>`;
        }

        // 3. Construction HTML de la carte
        li.innerHTML = `
            <div class="flex items-center flex-1 min-w-0 p-3" onclick="selectPersonnel('${person.id}')">
                <div class="w-10 h-10 rounded-[0.8rem] ${isSelected ? 'bg-white/20 border-transparent text-white' : `${avatarBg} ${avatarText} border ${avatarBorder}`} flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 mr-3 shadow-sm transition-colors">
                    <span class="text-xs font-black avatar-initials">${initials}</span>
                </div>
                
                <div class="flex flex-col min-w-0 flex-grow">
                    <p class="font-black text-sm uppercase tracking-tight truncate transition-colors ${nameColor}">
                        ${person.prenom} ${person.nom}
                    </p>
                    <p class="text-[9px] font-bold uppercase tracking-widest truncate mt-0.5 transition-colors ${infoColor}">
                        ${combinedInfo}
                    </p>
                </div>
            </div>
            
            <div class="personnel-actions flex items-center pr-3 shrink-0 gap-1">
                <button onclick="editPersonnel('${person.id}'); event.stopPropagation();" 
                    class="${btnClass} w-8 h-8 rounded-lg transition-all ${state.showArchived ? 'opacity-30 cursor-not-allowed' : ''}" 
                    title="${state.showArchived ? 'Impossible de modifier' : 'Modifier'}" 
                    ${state.showArchived || !canUserModify(person) ? 'disabled' : ''}>
                    <i class="fas fa-pencil-alt"></i>
                </button>
                ${actionBtn}
            </div>
        `;

        listElement.appendChild(li);
    });
}

/**
 * Gère la réactivation d'une personne archivée
 */
async function reactivatePersonnelHandler(personnelId) {
    const person = state.personnel.find(p => p.id === personnelId);
    if (!person) return;

    if (confirm(`Remettre en ligne ${person.prenom} ${person.nom} ?`)) {
        showLoader(true);
        try {
            const result = await serverCall('reactivatePersonnel', [personnelId]);
            if (result.error) throw new Error(result.error);
            
            showToast(`${person.prenom} a été remis en ligne.`, false);
            
            // On recharge les données
            await reloadAllData(); 
            
            // Si c'était le dernier archivé, on peut revenir à la vue active
            const remainingArchived = state.personnel.filter(p => p.statut === 'Archivé').length;
            if (remainingArchived === 0 && state.showArchived) {
                toggleArchiveView();
            }
        } catch(e) {
            showToast(`Erreur: ${e.message}`, true);
        } finally {
            hideLoader();
        }
    }
}
    
    function renderLegend() {
        elements.legendContainer.innerHTML = Object.entries(STATUSES).slice(1).map(([key, value]) => `<div class="flex items-center"><div class="w-4 h-4 rounded-full mr-2 status-bg-${key}"></div><span class="text-xs text-gray-500">${value}</span></div>`).join('');
    }

/**
 * Calcule et affiche les compteurs (CP, JRTT, Maladie, Longue Maladie, Formation) pour la vue individuelle
 */
function updateIndividualCounters() {
    const countersContainer = document.getElementById('individual-counters');
    if (!countersContainer) return;

    let countCP = 0;
    let countJRTT = 0;
    let countMaladie = 0;
    let countLongueMaladie = 0;
    let countFormation = 0;

    // On fouille dans les présences de l'année en cours
    for (const dateKey in state.presences) {
        const status = state.presences[dateKey].s;
        
        // Congés
        if (status === 'CP') countCP += 1;
        if (status === '4HCP') countCP += 0.5;
        
        // JRTT
        if (status === 'JRTT') countJRTT += 1;
        
        // Maladies (séparées)
        if (status === 'Ma') countMaladie += 1;
        if (status === 'LMa') countLongueMaladie += 1;
        
        // Formations
        if (status === 'F') countFormation += 1;
        if (status === '4HF') countFormation += 0.5;
    }

    // On dessine les 5 badges avec leurs icônes et couleurs adaptées
    countersContainer.innerHTML = `
        <div class="flex items-center gap-1.5 bg-emerald-50 border border-emerald-100 text-emerald-700 px-3 py-1 rounded-lg shadow-sm transition-all hover:scale-105">
            <i class="fas fa-sun text-[10px]"></i>
            <span class="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest">Congés : ${countCP}</span>
        </div>
        
        <div class="flex items-center gap-1.5 bg-teal-50 border border-teal-100 text-teal-700 px-3 py-1 rounded-lg shadow-sm transition-all hover:scale-105">
            <i class="fas fa-calendar-check text-[10px]"></i>
            <span class="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest">JRTT : ${countJRTT}</span>
        </div>
        
        <div class="flex items-center gap-1.5 bg-amber-50 border border-amber-100 text-amber-700 px-3 py-1 rounded-lg shadow-sm transition-all hover:scale-105">
            <i class="fas fa-graduation-cap text-[10px]"></i>
            <span class="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest">Format. : ${countFormation}</span>
        </div>
        
        <div class="flex items-center gap-1.5 bg-rose-50 border border-rose-100 text-rose-700 px-3 py-1 rounded-lg shadow-sm transition-all hover:scale-105">
            <i class="fas fa-stethoscope text-[10px]"></i>
            <span class="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest">Maladie : ${countMaladie}</span>
        </div>
        
        <div class="flex items-center gap-1.5 bg-red-50 border border-red-100 text-red-700 px-3 py-1 rounded-lg shadow-sm transition-all hover:scale-105">
            <i class="fas fa-hospital text-[10px]"></i>
            <span class="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest">Long. Mal. : ${countLongueMaladie}</span>
        </div>
    `;
}

function renderAnnualCalendar() {
    elements.calendarContainer.innerHTML = '';
    
    // 👇 AJOUTE CETTE LIGNE ICI :
    updateIndividualCounters();
    // Utilisation de la traduction dynamique
    const monthsFull = t('months_full').split(',');
    const daysMin = t('days_min').split(',');
    
    for (let month = 0; month < 12; month++) {
        const monthWrapper = document.createElement('div');
        monthWrapper.className = 'month-glass-card flex flex-col';
        monthWrapper.innerHTML = `<h3 class="font-black text-center mb-4 text-[#00205b] uppercase tracking-widest text-[11px]">${monthsFull[month]}</h3>`;
        
        const calendarGrid = document.createElement('div');
        calendarGrid.className = 'calendar';
        // Utilisation du tableau traduit (Correction de l'erreur de syntaxe ici !)
        daysMin.forEach(day => { calendarGrid.innerHTML += `<div class="day-header">${day}</div>`; });
        
        const firstDayOfMonth = new Date(Date.UTC(state.currentYear, month, 1));
        const lastDayOfMonth = new Date(Date.UTC(state.currentYear, month + 1, 0));
        
        const firstDayOfWeek = firstDayOfMonth.getUTCDay();
        let dayOffset = (firstDayOfWeek === 0) ? 6 : firstDayOfWeek - 1;

        for (let i = 0; i < dayOffset; i++) { calendarGrid.innerHTML += `<div></div>`; }
        
        for (let d = firstDayOfMonth; d <= lastDayOfMonth; d.setUTCDate(d.getUTCDate() + 1)) {
            const originalDateKey = d.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
            const day = d.getUTCDate(); 
            
            const dayData = state.presences[originalDateKey] || {};
            const status = dayData.s || '';
            const comment = dayData.c || '';
            const hs = dayData.hs || 0; // ✨ NOUVEAU : Lecture des Heures Supplémentaires
            
            const isHoliday = state.holidays[state.currentYear] && state.holidays[state.currentYear][originalDateKey];
            
            let circleClasses = 'calendar-day-circle';
            let dayContent = day;
            
            let titleText = '';
            if (comment) {
                titleText = comment;
            } else if (isHoliday) {
                titleText = state.holidays[state.currentYear][originalDateKey];
            }
            const titleAttr = titleText ? `title="${titleText.replace(/"/g, '&quot;')}"` : '';

            if (status) {
                circleClasses += ` status-bg-${status}`;
                dayContent = t_abbr(status); // ICI : On affiche l'abréviation traduite
            } else if (isHoliday) {
                circleClasses += ' weekend-day';
            } else if (d.getUTCDay() === 0 || d.getUTCDay() === 6) {
                circleClasses += ' weekend-day';
            }
            
            const commentDotHtml = comment ? `<span class="notification-dot z-10" title="${comment.replace(/"/g, '&quot;')}"></span>` : '';
            
            // ✨ NOUVEAU : Génération de la pastille HS pour le calendrier annuel (plus petite pour s'adapter)
            let hsBadgeHtml = '';
            if (hs !== 0) {
                const sign = hs > 0 ? '+' : '';
                const hsColor = hs > 0 ? 'bg-[#00205b]' : 'bg-red-500';
                hsBadgeHtml = `<span class="absolute -bottom-1 -left-1 ${hsColor} text-white text-[7px] font-black px-1 py-0.5 rounded shadow-sm border border-white z-20 leading-none pointer-events-none">${sign}${hs}h</span>`;
            }
            
            calendarGrid.innerHTML += `
                <div class="calendar-day-wrapper" ${titleAttr} onclick="openEditor(event, '${originalDateKey}')">
                    <div class="${circleClasses}">${dayContent}</div>
                    ${commentDotHtml}
                    ${hsBadgeHtml}
                </div>`;
        }
        
        monthWrapper.appendChild(calendarGrid);
        elements.calendarContainer.appendChild(monthWrapper);
    }
}

/**
 * [NOUVEAU] Met à jour dynamiquement toutes les listes déroulantes de rôles dans la modale.
 */
function _updateRoleDropdowns() {
    const rolesList = document.getElementById('settings-roles-list');
    const availableRoles = Array.from(rolesList.querySelectorAll('li')).map(li => li.dataset.role);
    
const roleOptionsHtml = [
        `<option value="Administrateur">${t_role('Administrateur')}</option>`,
        ...availableRoles.map(r => `<option value="${r}">${t_role(r)}</option>`),
        `<option value="Lecteur">${t_role('Lecteur')}</option>`
    ].join('');

    // Met à jour le sélecteur pour l'ajout de nouveaux utilisateurs
    document.getElementById('setting-new-user-role').innerHTML = roleOptionsHtml;

    // Met à jour tous les sélecteurs existants dans la liste des utilisateurs
    document.querySelectorAll('#settings-roles-assignments-list select').forEach(select => {
        const currentValue = select.value;
        select.innerHTML = roleOptionsHtml;
        select.value = currentValue; // On essaie de préserver la valeur sélectionnée
    });
}

/**
 * [AMÉLIORÉ] Ajoute un rôle à la liste UI avec des contrôles de validité.
 */
function addRoleToSettingsList() {
    const input = document.getElementById('setting-new-role');
    const roleName = input.value.trim();
    
    if (!roleName) {
        showToast("Le nom du rôle ne peut pas être vide.", true);
        return;
    }
    
    const existingRoles = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#settings-roles-list li')).map(li => li.dataset.role.toLowerCase());
    if (existingRoles.includes(roleName.toLowerCase())) {
        showToast("Ce rôle existe déjà.", true);
        return;
    }

    const list = document.getElementById('settings-roles-list');
    const li = document.createElement('li');
    li.className = 'flex items-center justify-between bg-white p-2 rounded-md shadow-sm';
    li.dataset.role = roleName;
    li.innerHTML = `<span>${roleName}</span>
                    <button type="button" onclick="this.parentElement.remove(); _updateRoleDropdowns();" class="text-red-400 hover:text-red-600 w-8 h-8 rounded-full hover:bg-red-100 transition-all" title="Supprimer">&times;</button>`;
    list.appendChild(li);
    input.value = '';
    input.focus();

    // On met à jour les listes déroulantes instantanément
    _updateRoleDropdowns(); 
}
function addMissionToSettingsList() {
    const nameInput = document.getElementById('setting-new-mission-name');
    const colorSelect = document.getElementById('setting-new-mission-color');
    const name = nameInput.value.trim();
    const color = colorSelect.value;
    
    if (!name) return showToast("Le nom de la mission ne peut pas être vide.", true);
    
    const existingMissions = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#settings-missions-list li')).map(li => li.dataset.nom.toLowerCase());
    if (existingMissions.includes(name.toLowerCase())) return showToast("Cette mission existe déjà.", true);

    const list = document.getElementById('settings-missions-list');
    const li = document.createElement('li');
    li.className = `flex items-center justify-between p-2.5 rounded-xl shadow-sm border border-white ${color}`;
    li.dataset.nom = name;
    li.dataset.color = color;
    li.innerHTML = `
        <span class="font-black text-[11px] uppercase tracking-widest ml-2">${name}</span>
        <button type="button" onclick="this.parentElement.remove();" class="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-white/50 hover:bg-red-100 hover:text-red-600 transition-all flex items-center justify-center" title="Supprimer">&times;</button>
    `;
    list.appendChild(li);
    
    nameInput.value = '';
    nameInput.focus();
}

/**
 * Alterne entre la vue groupée (par poste/REAP) et la vue liste plate alphabétique.
 */
function toggleFlatView() {
    state.isFlatView = !state.isFlatView;
    
    const btnText = document.getElementById('toggle-flat-view-text');
    const btnIcon = document.querySelector('#toggle-flat-view-btn i');

    if (state.isFlatView) {
        btnText.textContent = "VUE GROUPÉE";
        btnIcon.className = "fas fa-layer-group text-[#00b5e2] text-lg mr-3 group-hover:text-white transition-colors";
        showToast("Affichage en liste simple (Tri alphabétique)", false);
    } else {
        btnText.textContent = "VUE LISTE";
        btnIcon.className = "fas fa-list text-[#00b5e2] text-lg mr-3 group-hover:text-white transition-colors";
        showToast("Affichage groupé par sections activé", false);
    }
    
    // On redessine le tableau avec le nouveau mode
    renderTeamViewTable(state.teamPresences, state.currentTeamPersonnel);
}

/**
 * Alterne entre le tri par Nom et par Prénom pour la vue équipe.
 */
function toggleTeamSort() {
    state.teamSortMode = (state.teamSortMode === 'nom') ? 'prenom' : 'nom';
    const label = state.teamSortMode === 'nom' ? t('sort_name') : t('sort_firstname');
    showToast(`${t('toast_sort_by')} ${label}`);
    renderTeamViewTable(state.teamPresences, state.currentTeamPersonnel);
}
    
// ATTENTION: Cette fonction écrase l'ancienne, elle construit l'en-tête (le header)
function renderTeamViewTable(teamPresences, personnelForView) {
    try {
        const [year, month] = state.teamViewDate.split('-').map(Number);
        const daysInMonth = new Date(year, month, 0).getDate();
        const weekDays = t('days_short').split(',');

        let filteredPersonnel = personnelForView || [];
        if (state.workstationFilter && state.workstationFilter.length > 0) {
            filteredPersonnel = filteredPersonnel.filter(p => {
                if (!p.posteDeTravail) return false;
                const pWs = p.posteDeTravail.split(',').map(s => s.trim());
                return state.workstationFilter.some(selectedWs => pWs.includes(selectedWs));
            });
        }

        const headerContainer = document.getElementById('team-view-header-container');
        const bodyContainer = document.getElementById('team-view-body-container');
        const currentHeader = headerContainer.querySelector('th:last-child');
        const daysInHeader = currentHeader ? parseInt(currentHeader.textContent) : 0;
        const monthHasChanged = !headerContainer.innerHTML || daysInHeader !== daysInMonth;

        if (monthHasChanged) {
            let headerTableHtml = '<table class="w-full text-left text-sm whitespace-nowrap table-fixed"><thead><tr>';
            headerTableHtml += `
                <th class="sticky left-0 z-20 p-4 text-left modern-th" style="width: 280px; min-width: 280px;">
                    <div class="flex items-center justify-between gap-2">
                        <span class="text-xs font-black tracking-[0.2em] text-[#00205b] uppercase">${t('table_personnel')}</span>
                        <button onclick="toggleTeamSort()" class="inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2.5 py-1 bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg shadow-sm hover:border-[#00b5e2] transition-all focus:outline-none group" title="${t('sort_by_tooltip')} ${state.teamSortMode === 'nom' ? t('sort_firstname') : t('sort_name')}">
                            <i class="fas fa-sort-alpha-down text-xs text-gray-400 group-hover:text-[#00b5e2]"></i>
                            <span class="text-[9px] uppercase font-black text-gray-500 group-hover:text-[#00b5e2]">${state.teamSortMode === 'nom' ? t('sort_name') : t('sort_firstname')}</span>
                        </button>
                    </div>
                </th>`;
            
            for (let i = 1; i <= daysInMonth; i++) {
                const d = new Date(Date.UTC(year, month - 1, i));
                const dayOfWeek = weekDays[d.getUTCDay()];
                const isWeekend = d.getUTCDay() === 0 || d.getUTCDay() === 6;
                headerTableHtml += `
                    <th class="text-center p-2 modern-th border-l border-white/50" style="width: 46px; min-width: 46px;">
                        <div class="text-[9px] font-black tracking-widest uppercase ${isWeekend ? 'text-red-400' : 'text-gray-400'}">${dayOfWeek}</div>
                        <div class="text-sm font-black ${isWeekend ? 'text-red-500' : 'text-[#00205b]'}">${i}</div>
                    </th>`;
            }
            headerTableHtml += '</tr></thead></table>';
            headerContainer.innerHTML = headerTableHtml;
            bodyContainer.innerHTML = '<table class="w-full text-left text-sm whitespace-nowrap table-fixed"><tbody id="team-view-tbody"></tbody></table>';
        }

        const tableBody = bodyContainer.querySelector('#team-view-tbody');
        if (!tableBody) return;

        const isGroupByMachine = state.isFlatView ? false : (state.settings && state.settings.groupByMachine);
const personnelGrouped = {};
filteredPersonnel.forEach(p => {
    let groupId = 'SANS_GROUPE';
    
    // NOUVELLE LOGIQUE QUI GÈRE LA VUE LISTE PLATE
    if (state.isFlatView) {
        groupId = 'TOUS'; // Un seul groupe pour tout le monde
    } else if (isGroupByMachine) {
        groupId = p.posteDeTravail ? p.posteDeTravail.split(',')[0].trim() : t('table_unassigned');
    } else {
        groupId = p.chefEquipeAssocie || 'NO_REAP';
    }
    
    if (!personnelGrouped[groupId]) personnelGrouped[groupId] = [];
    personnelGrouped[groupId].push(p);
});

        const groupIds = Object.keys(personnelGrouped);
        groupIds.sort((a, b) => {
            if (isGroupByMachine) return a.localeCompare(b);
            const reapA = state.personnel.find(p => p.id === a);
            const reapB = state.personnel.find(p => p.id === b);
            return (reapA ? `${reapA.prenom} ${reapA.nom}` : '').localeCompare(reapB ? `${reapB.prenom} ${reapB.nom}` : '');
        });

        const existingRows = new Map();
        tableBody.querySelectorAll('tr[data-person-id]').forEach(row => existingRows.set(row.dataset.personId, row));
        tableBody.querySelectorAll('.machine-separator').forEach(row => row.remove());

        let lastAppendedRow = null;
  
  // --- NOUVEAU : Rendu asynchrone par lots (Chunking) ---
  let currentGroupIndex = 0;
  let currentPersonIndex = 0;
  const CHUNK_SIZE = 25; // Nombre de personnes dessinées par "rafale"

  function renderNextChunk() {
    let processedThisFrame = 0;

    while (currentGroupIndex < groupIds.length && processedThisFrame < CHUNK_SIZE) {
      const groupId = groupIds[currentGroupIndex];
      // On récupère et on trie les personnes du groupe (identique à ton code actuel)
const personsInGroup = [...personnelGrouped[groupId]].sort((a, b) => {
    
    // --- NOUVEAU : Si Vue Liste activée, on zappe les postes/quarts et on fait un tri 100% alphabétique ! ---
    if (state.isFlatView) {
        return state.teamSortMode === 'prenom' ?
            (a.prenom || "").localeCompare(b.prenom || "") :
            (a.nom || "").localeCompare(b.nom || "");
    }

    // --- Reste de la logique normale pour la vue groupée ---
    if (isGroupByMachine) {
        const order = { 'M': 1, 'A': 2, 'N': 3, 'J': 4 };
        const qA = order[a.quartDefaut] || 5;
        const qB = order[b.quartDefaut] || 5;
        if (qA !== qB) return qA - qB;
    } else {
        const comparePoste = (a.posteDeTravail || "").localeCompare(b.posteDeTravail || "");
        if (comparePoste !== 0) return comparePoste;
    }
    
    return state.teamSortMode === 'prenom' ?
        (a.prenom || "").localeCompare(b.prenom || "") :
        (a.nom || "").localeCompare(b.nom || "");
});

      // Gestion du séparateur de Machine (uniquement au début du groupe)
      if (isGroupByMachine && currentPersonIndex === 0) {
        const separatorRow = document.createElement('tr');
        separatorRow.className = 'machine-separator';
        let separatorHtml = `<td class="sticky left-0 z-20 bg-[#00205b] text-white font-black uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-[10px] py-1.5 px-4 border-y-2 border-white shadow-sm" style="width: 280px; min-width: 280px; max-width: 280px;">
          <div class="flex items-center gap-2 truncate">
                            <i class="fas fa-industry text-[#00b5e2]"></i> ${t('table_machine')}: ${groupId}
                        </div></td>`;
        for (let i = 0; i < daysInMonth; i++) {
          separatorHtml += `<td class="bg-[#00205b] border-y-2 border-white opacity-40" style="width: 46px; min-width: 46px;"></td>`;
        }
        separatorRow.innerHTML = separatorHtml;
        if (lastAppendedRow) tableBody.insertBefore(separatorRow, lastAppendedRow.nextSibling);
        else tableBody.appendChild(separatorRow);
        lastAppendedRow = separatorRow;
      }

      // Boucle sur les personnes du groupe pour ce lot
      while (currentPersonIndex < personsInGroup.length && processedThisFrame < CHUNK_SIZE) {
        const person = personsInGroup[currentPersonIndex];
        const dateKeys = Array.from({ length: daysInMonth }, (_, i) => `${year}-${String(month).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(i + 1).padStart(2, '0')}`);
        const isGroupStart = !state.isFlatView && !isGroupByMachine && currentPersonIndex === 0;

        // --- Logique de création/mise à jour de la ligne (identique à ton code) ---
        if (existingRows.has(person.id)) {
          const row = existingRows.get(person.id);
          const nameCell = row.querySelector('td');
          if (nameCell) nameCell.outerHTML = buildNameCellHtml(person, isGroupByMachine, isGroupStart);
          dateKeys.forEach(dateKey => updateTeamViewCell(row, person.id, dateKey));
          existingRows.delete(person.id);
          if (lastAppendedRow) tableBody.insertBefore(row, lastAppendedRow.nextSibling);
          else tableBody.appendChild(row);
          lastAppendedRow = row;
        } else {
          const newRow = document.createElement('tr');
          newRow.className = 'modern-tr border-b border-gray-100/50';
          newRow.dataset.personId = person.id;
          let rowHtml = buildNameCellHtml(person, isGroupByMachine, isGroupStart);
          dateKeys.forEach(dateKey => rowHtml += buildDayCellHtml(person.id, dateKey));
          newRow.innerHTML = rowHtml;
          if (lastAppendedRow) tableBody.insertBefore(newRow, lastAppendedRow.nextSibling);
          else tableBody.appendChild(newRow);
          lastAppendedRow = newRow;
        }
        // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

        currentPersonIndex++;
        processedThisFrame++;
      }

      // Passage au groupe suivant si on a fini celui-ci
      if (currentPersonIndex >= personsInGroup.length) {
        currentGroupIndex++;
        currentPersonIndex = 0;
      }
    }

    // A-t-on tout fini ?
    if (currentGroupIndex < groupIds.length) {
      // Non, on laisse le navigateur respirer et on rappelle la fonction pour la suite
      setTimeout(renderNextChunk, 15);
    } else {
      // Oui, on termine le traitement !
      existingRows.forEach(row => row.remove());
      updateTeamViewTotals(filteredPersonnel, daysInMonth, year, month);
      
      // Gestion de la scrollbar (identique à ton code)
      bodyContainer.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        headerContainer.scrollLeft = bodyContainer.scrollLeft;
      });
      setTimeout(() => {
        const scrollbarWidth = bodyContainer.offsetWidth - bodyContainer.clientWidth;
        headerContainer.style.paddingRight = `${scrollbarWidth}px`;
      }, 0);
    }
  }

  // On lance la machine
  renderNextChunk();

} catch (e) {
  console.error('Erreur renderTeamViewTable: ', e);
  }
}

function setupTeamViewWorkstationFilter() {
    const optionsContainer = document.getElementById('ws-filter-options');
    const buttonText = document.getElementById('ws-filter-text');
    if (!optionsContainer) return;

    // Récupère uniquement les postes présents dans l'équipe actuellement affichée
    const uniqueWs = new Set();
    (state.currentTeamPersonnel || []).forEach(p => {
        if (p.posteDeTravail) {
            p.posteDeTravail.split(',').forEach(ws => uniqueWs.add(ws.trim()));
        }
    });
    const wsArray = Array.from(uniqueWs).filter(Boolean).sort();

    // Design des options amélioré (avec traduction)
    let html = `
        <label class="flex items-center px-4 py-3 cursor-pointer rounded-xl hover:bg-gray-50 transition-colors mb-1 group">
            <input type="checkbox" value="Tous" class="ws-filter-cb h-4 w-4 text-[#00b5e2] border-gray-300 rounded focus:ring-[#00b5e2] cursor-pointer" ${state.workstationFilter.length === 0 ? 'checked' : ''}>
            <span class="ml-3 text-[11px] font-black text-[#00205b] uppercase tracking-widest group-hover:text-[#00b5e2] transition-colors">${t('filter_all_workstations')}</span>
        </label>
        <div class="h-px w-full bg-gray-100 my-1"></div>
    `;

    wsArray.forEach(ws => {
        const isChecked = state.workstationFilter.includes(ws);
        html += `
            <label class="flex items-center px-4 py-2.5 cursor-pointer rounded-xl hover:bg-gray-50 transition-colors mb-1 group">
                <input type="checkbox" value="${ws}" class="ws-filter-cb h-4 w-4 text-[#00205b] border-gray-300 rounded focus:ring-[#00b5e2] cursor-pointer" ${isChecked ? 'checked' : ''}>
                <span class="ml-3 text-[11px] font-bold text-gray-600 uppercase tracking-widest group-hover:text-[#00205b] transition-colors">${ws}</span>
            </label>
        `;
    });

    optionsContainer.innerHTML = html;

    // Gestion du clic sur les cases
    const checkboxes = optionsContainer.querySelectorAll('.ws-filter-cb');
    checkboxes.forEach(cb => {
        cb.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            const val = e.target.value;
            if (val === 'Tous') {
                if (e.target.checked) {
                    state.workstationFilter = [];
                    checkboxes.forEach(c => { if(c.value !== 'Tous') c.checked = false; });
                } else {
                    e.target.checked = true; // Empêche de décocher "Tous" si rien n'est sélectionné
                }
            } else {
                optionsContainer.querySelector('input[value="Tous"]').checked = false;
                const selected = Array.from(checkboxes).filter(c => c.checked && c.value !== 'Tous').map(c => c.value);
                state.workstationFilter = selected;
                
                if (selected.length === 0) {
                    optionsContainer.querySelector('input[value="Tous"]').checked = true;
                }
            }

            // Met à jour le texte et la couleur du bouton principal (avec traduction)
            if (state.workstationFilter.length === 0) {
                buttonText.textContent = t('filter_all_workstations');
                buttonText.classList.remove('text-[#00b5e2]');
                buttonText.classList.add('text-[#00205b]');
            } else {
                buttonText.textContent = `${state.workstationFilter.length} ${t('filter_selected_workstations')}`;
                buttonText.classList.remove('text-[#00205b]');
                buttonText.classList.add('text-[#00b5e2]');
            }

            // Recharge le tableau localement (instantané)
            renderTeamViewTable(state.teamPresences, state.currentTeamPersonnel);
        });
    });
}

function buildNameCellHtml(person, isGroupByMachine = false, isGroupStart = false) {
    const isHighlighted = getHighlightedIDs().includes(person.id);
    let roleInitialContent = '', roleInitialClasses = 'inline-flex items-center justify-center h-6 w-6 rounded-lg text-[10px] font-black mr-3 shrink-0', roleInitialTitle = t_role(person.role);
    
    if (person.role === 'Compagnon') { roleInitialContent = 'C'; roleInitialClasses += ' bg-sky-100 text-sky-600 border border-sky-200'; }
    else if (person.role === 'Intérimaire') { roleInitialContent = 'I'; roleInitialClasses += ' bg-fuchsia-100 text-fuchsia-600 border border-fuchsia-200'; }
    else if (person.role === 'RP') { roleInitialContent = 'RP'; roleInitialClasses += ' bg-purple-100 text-purple-700 border border-purple-300'; }
    else if (person.role === 'REAP') { roleInitialContent = 'RE'; roleInitialClasses += ' bg-emerald-100 text-emerald-700 border border-emerald-300'; }
    else if (person.role === 'Pilote') { roleInitialContent = 'P'; roleInitialClasses += ' bg-blue-100 text-blue-700 border border-blue-300'; }
    else { roleInitialContent = person.role.charAt(0); roleInitialClasses += ' bg-gray-100 text-gray-600 border border-gray-200'; }
    
    const roleInitialSpan = roleInitialContent ? `<span class="${roleInitialClasses}" title="${roleInitialTitle}">${roleInitialContent}</span>` : '';

    const tauxBadge = (person.tauxEfficacite && person.tauxEfficacite < 100) ? 
        `<span class="ml-2 bg-orange-100 text-orange-600 text-[9px] font-black px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded shadow-sm border border-orange-200">${person.tauxEfficacite}%</span>` : '';

    const infoParts = [person.posteDeTravail, person.section ? `Sec. ${person.section}` : null].filter(Boolean);
    const combinedInfo = infoParts.length > 0 ? infoParts.join(' • ') : 'Non assigné';

    let rowBgClass = isHighlighted ? 'bg-blue-50 border-l-4 border-l-[#00b5e2]' : 'bg-white border-l-4 border-l-transparent';
    let shiftBadge = '';
    
    if (isGroupByMachine) {
        const quart = person.quartDefaut || 'J';
        if (quart === 'M') {
            rowBgClass = 'bg-[#f3e8ff] border-l-8 border-l-[#9333ea]'; 
            shiftBadge = '<span class="ml-2 bg-[#9333ea] text-white text-[8.5px] font-black px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded shadow-sm">MATIN</span>';
        } else if (quart === 'A') {
            rowBgClass = 'bg-[#fef08a] border-l-8 border-l-[#eab308]'; 
            shiftBadge = '<span class="ml-2 bg-[#eab308] text-[#00205b] text-[8.5px] font-black px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded shadow-sm">APREM</span>';
        } else if (quart === 'N') {
            rowBgClass = 'bg-[#bbf7d0] border-l-8 border-l-[#22c55e]'; 
            shiftBadge = '<span class="ml-2 bg-[#22c55e] text-[#00205b] text-[8.5px] font-black px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded shadow-sm">NUIT</span>';
        }
    } else if (isGroupStart) {
        rowBgClass += ' reap-group-start';
    }

    // 🔴 LA CORRECTION EST ICI : min-w-0 ajouté au flex pour protéger la largeur !
    return `<td class="sticky left-0 z-10 py-3 px-4 modern-td-name cursor-pointer ${rowBgClass}" style="width: 280px; min-width: 280px; max-width: 280px;" title="${person.prenom} ${person.nom} • ${person.matricule}" oncontextmenu="toggleNameHighlight(event, '${person.id}')">
        <div class="flex items-center w-full min-w-0">
            ${roleInitialSpan}
            <div class="truncate flex-grow min-w-0">
                <p class="text-xs font-black text-[#00205b] uppercase truncate tracking-tight leading-none mb-1">${person.nom} <span class="font-bold text-gray-400">${person.prenom}</span> ${shiftBadge} ${tauxBadge}</p>
                <p class="text-[10px] font-bold text-[#00b5e2] tracking-widest truncate uppercase">${combinedInfo}</p>
            </div>
        </div>
    </td>`;
}

function buildDayCellHtml(personnelId, dateKey) {
    const dayData = (state.teamPresences[personnelId] && state.teamPresences[personnelId][dateKey]) || {};
    const status = dayData.s || '';
    const comment = dayData.c || '';
    const hs = dayData.hs || 0;
    const loc = dayData.loc || ''; // <-- NOUVEAU : ON RÉCUPÈRE LE LIEU DE MISSION
    
    const [year, month, day] = dateKey.split('-').map(Number);
    const d = new Date(Date.UTC(year, month - 1, day));
    
    const isWeekend = d.getUTCDay() === 0 || d.getUTCDay() === 6;
    const isHoliday = state.holidays[year] && state.holidays[year][dateKey];

    let titleAttribute = comment ? `title="${comment.replace(/"/g, '&quot;')}"` : (isHoliday ? `title="${state.holidays[year][dateKey]}"` : '');
    const commentDotHtml = comment ? `<span class="absolute -top-1 -right-1 w-2.5 h-2.5 bg-[#00b5e2] border-2 border-white rounded-full z-10"></span>` : '';
    
    let hsBadgeHtml = '';
    if (hs !== 0) {
        const sign = hs > 0 ? '+' : '';
        const hsColor = hs > 0 ? 'bg-[#00205b]' : 'bg-red-500';
        hsBadgeHtml = `<span class="absolute -bottom-1.5 -left-1.5 ${hsColor} text-white text-[8px] font-black px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-md shadow-md border border-white z-20 leading-none">${sign}${hs}h</span>`;
    }
    
    let cellBgClass = 'border-l border-gray-100';
    if (!status && isHoliday) cellBgClass += ' bg-gray-200';
    else if (!status && isWeekend) cellBgClass += ' bg-red-50';
    else cellBgClass += ' bg-white';

    // --- NOUVEAU : GESTION DE LA MISSION DYNAMIQUE ---
    let extraClasses = `status-bg-${status}`;
    let missionBadgeHtml = '';

    if (status === 'Mi') {
        let missionColorClass = 'bg-mission-defaut'; // Couleur grise par défaut

        // On cherche la mission dans les paramètres pour trouver sa couleur
        if (state.settings && state.settings.missions) {
            const foundMission = state.settings.missions.find(m => m.nom.toLowerCase() === loc.toLowerCase());
            if (foundMission) {
                missionColorClass = foundMission.colorClass;
            }
        }
        
        extraClasses = missionColorClass;

        if (loc) {
            const shortLoc = loc.substring(0, 2).toUpperCase();
            missionBadgeHtml = `<span class="absolute -top-1 -left-1 bg-white/90 backdrop-blur-sm text-[6px] font-black px-[3px] py-[1px] rounded-[4px] shadow-sm border border-gray-200 z-20 leading-none" style="color: inherit;">${shortLoc}</span>`;
        }
    }
    // ----------------------------------------

return `
        <td id="cell-${personnelId}-${dateKey}" class="p-1 cursor-pointer hover:bg-gray-100 ${cellBgClass}" style="width: 46px; min-width: 46px;" ${titleAttribute} onclick="openEditor(event, '${dateKey}', '${personnelId}')">
            <div class="relative w-7 h-7 mx-auto">
                <div class="team-view-cell w-full h-full ${extraClasses}">${t_abbr(status)}</div> ${commentDotHtml}
                ${hsBadgeHtml}
                ${missionBadgeHtml} 
            </div>
        </td>`;
}

/**
 * Met à jour une cellule de jour spécifique déjà affichée à l'écran.
 * @param {HTMLElement} rowElement - L'élément <tr> de la ligne à mettre à jour.
 * @param {string} personnelId - L'ID de la personne.
 * @param {string} dateKey - La date de la cellule à mettre à jour.
 */
function updateTeamViewCell(rowElement, personnelId, dateKey) {
    const cell = rowElement.querySelector(`#cell-${personnelId}-${dateKey}`);
    if (!cell) return;
    
    // On reconstruit juste le HTML de la cellule et on le remplace.
    cell.outerHTML = buildDayCellHtml(personnelId, dateKey);
}

async function openSettingsModal() {
    if (!state.settings) {
        showToast("Les paramètres ne sont pas encore chargés.", true);
        return;
    }
    document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
    document.getElementById('settings-modal').classList.remove('hidden');
    
    // 1. Chargement des paramètres généraux existants
    document.getElementById('setting-app-name').value = state.settings.appName || '';
    document.getElementById('setting-workstations').value = (state.settings.workstations || []).join('\n');

    // Charge l'état du bouton Vue Machine
    const groupMachineCb = document.getElementById('setting-group-machine');
    if (groupMachineCb) groupMachineCb.checked = state.settings.groupByMachine || false;

    // 👇 AJOUT : On sélectionne le bon pays dans les paramètres
    const holidayCountry = state.settings.holidayCountry || 'FR';
    const countryRadio = document.querySelector(`input[name="holiday_country"][value="${holidayCountry}"]`);
    if (countryRadio) countryRadio.checked = true;
    // ☝️ FIN DE L'AJOUT

    // 2. Chargement de la liste des rôles
    const rolesList = document.getElementById('settings-roles-list');
    rolesList.innerHTML = '';
    
    (state.settings.roles || []).forEach(roleName => {
        const li = document.createElement('li');
        li.className = 'flex items-center justify-between bg-white p-2 rounded-md shadow-sm';
        li.dataset.role = roleName;
        li.innerHTML = '<span class="translated-role">' + t_role(roleName) + '</span>' +
        '<button type="button" onclick="this.parentElement.remove(); _updateRoleDropdowns();" class="text-red-400 hover:text-red-600 w-8 h-8 rounded-full hover:bg-red-100 transition-all" title="Supprimer">&times;</button>';
        rolesList.appendChild(li);
    });

    const missionsList = document.getElementById('settings-missions-list');
    if (missionsList) {
        missionsList.innerHTML = '';
        (state.settings.missions || []).forEach(mission => {
            const li = document.createElement('li');
            li.className = 'flex items-center justify-between p-2.5 rounded-xl shadow-sm border border-white ' + mission.colorClass;
            li.dataset.nom = mission.nom;
            li.dataset.color = mission.colorClass;
            li.innerHTML = '<span class="font-black text-[11px] uppercase tracking-widest ml-2">' + mission.nom + '</span>' +
            '<button type="button" onclick="this.parentElement.remove();" class="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-white/50 hover:bg-red-100 hover:text-red-600 transition-all flex items-center justify-center" title="Supprimer">&times;</button>';
            missionsList.appendChild(li);
        });
    }

    const exportContainer = document.getElementById('export-roles-container');
    if (exportContainer && state.settings.roles) {
        exportContainer.innerHTML = state.settings.roles.map(role => 
            '<label class="flex items-center gap-3 p-3 bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl cursor-pointer hover:border-emerald-300 hover:bg-emerald-50 transition-all shadow-sm group">' +
                '<input type="checkbox" value="' + role + '" class="export-role-cb h-5 w-5 text-emerald-500 border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:ring-emerald-500 transition-all">' +
                '<span class="translated-role text-[11px] font-black text-gray-600 group-hover:text-emerald-800 uppercase tracking-wider">' + t_role(role) + '</span>' +
            '</label>'
        ).join('');
    }

    const targetModeSelect = document.getElementById('setting-target-mode');
    if (targetModeSelect) {
        targetModeSelect.value = state.settings.targetMode || 'auto';
    }

    serverCall('getRoleAssignments').then(assignments => {
        populateRoleAssignmentsUI(assignments);
    }).catch(e => console.error("Erreur chargement accès:", e));

    serverCall('getAvailableCapaStations').then(availableStations => {
        window.availableFileStations = availableStations || [];
        const capaContainer = document.getElementById('capa-stations-list');
        const savedStations = state.settings.capaWorkstations || [];
        const appWorkstations = state.settings.workstations || [];
        
        if (!appWorkstations || appWorkstations.length === 0) {
            capaContainer.innerHTML = '<p class="text-sm text-red-500 col-span-full">Veuillez d\'abord configurer vos postes de travail dans l\'onglet Général.</p>';
        } else {
            capaContainer.innerHTML = appWorkstations.map(st => 
                '<label class="relative cursor-pointer group">' +
                    '<input type="checkbox" value="' + st + '" class="capa-station-cb peer sr-only" ' + (savedStations.includes(st) ? 'checked' : '') + ' onchange="window.renderCapaRuleCards && window.renderCapaRuleCards()">' +
                    '<div class="flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-white border-2 border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm transition-all duration-300 peer-checked:border-[#00b5e2] peer-checked:bg-[#00b5e2]/5 peer-checked:shadow-md group-hover:border-[#00b5e2]/40 group-hover:shadow-md">' +
                        '<div class="flex items-center gap-3 overflow-hidden">' +
                            '<div class="w-8 h-8 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 transition-colors duration-300 shadow-inner bg-gray-50 text-gray-400 peer-checked:bg-[#00b5e2] peer-checked:text-white">' +
                                '<i class="fas fa-layer-group text-xs"></i>' +
                            '</div>' +
                            '<span class="text-[11px] font-black uppercase text-[#00205b] truncate transition-colors duration-300 peer-checked:text-[#00b5e2] tracking-widest">' + st + '</span>' +
                        '</div>' +
                        '<div class="w-5 h-5 rounded-full border-2 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 transition-all duration-300 border-gray-200 peer-checked:border-[#00b5e2] peer-checked:bg-[#00b5e2]">' +
                            '<i class="fas fa-check text-white text-[9px] opacity-0 scale-50 transition-all duration-300 peer-checked:opacity-100 peer-checked:scale-100"></i>' +
                        '</div>' +
                    '</div>' +
                '</label>'
            ).join('');
            if(window.renderCapaRuleCards) window.renderCapaRuleCards();
        }
    }).catch(e => console.error("Erreur chargement cibles CAPA:", e));
}

window.renderCapaRuleCards = () => {
    const selectedStations = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.capa-station-cb:checked')).map(cb => cb.value);
    const container = document.getElementById('capa-rules-container');
    const targetModeSelect = document.getElementById('setting-target-mode');
    const targetMode = targetModeSelect ? targetModeSelect.value : (state.settings.targetMode || 'auto');
    
    if (selectedStations.length === 0) {
        container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-xs text-gray-400 italic text-center py-6 bg-slate-50 rounded-2xl border border-dashed border-gray-200 xl:col-span-2">Cochez des postes ci-dessus pour les configurer.</p>';
        return;
    }
    
    let htmlCards = '';
    
    // On récupère TOUS les postes définis dans l'onglet Général pour créer nos cases à cocher
    const allWorkstations = state.settings.workstations || [];

    selectedStations.forEach(station => {
        const rule = (state.settings.capaRules && state.settings.capaRules[station]) || { 
            calcMode: 'theorique', cycle: '2x8', maxStaffDay: 18, maxCapDay: 1.9, 
            maxStaffNight: 9, maxCapNight: 1.2, mapping: '', prodTime: 10, trs: 100 
        };
        const is3x8 = rule.cycle === '3x8';
        const isReel = rule.calcMode === 'reel';
        const trsValue = rule.trs !== undefined ? rule.trs : 100;
        
        // Liste des postes inclus dans la fusion pour CE poste
        const includedStationsList = (rule.includedStations || station).split(',').map(s => s.trim());

        const fileOptionsHtml = (window.availableFileStations || []).map(s => 
            '<option value="' + s + '"' + (rule.mapping === s ? ' selected' : '') + '>' + s + '</option>'
        ).join('');

        let manualWeeksHtml = '';
        for (let w = 1; w <= 52; w++) {
            let weekValue = (state.settings.manualTargets && state.settings.manualTargets[station] && state.settings.manualTargets[station][w] !== undefined) 
                ? state.settings.manualTargets[station][w] 
                : 10;
            manualWeeksHtml += '<div class="flex flex-col items-center">' +
                '<span class="text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-500 mb-1">S' + w + '</span>' +
                '<input type="number" step="0.1" data-week="' + w + '" class="rule-manual-target-week w-full glass-input bg-white border border-purple-200 rounded-lg p-1 text-sm text-center font-black text-[#00205b] outline-none focus:border-purple-400 transition-all shadow-sm" value="' + weekValue + '">' +
                '</div>';
        }

        let targetModeSection = '';
        if (targetMode === 'auto') {
            targetModeSection = '<div class="bg-gray-50/80 p-4 rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 mt-2">' +
                '<label class="text-[9px] font-black text-gray-600 uppercase tracking-widest mb-2 flex items-center gap-2"><i class="fas fa-link text-[#00b5e2]"></i> Source des objectifs</label>' +
                '<select class="rule-mapping w-full glass-input bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-4 py-2 text-xs font-bold text-[#00205b] outline-none focus:border-[#00b5e2] transition-all cursor-pointer">' +
                fileOptionsHtml +
                '<option value="">-- Aucun lien --</option>' +
                '</select></div>';
        } else {
            targetModeSection = '<div class="bg-purple-50/80 p-5 rounded-2xl border border-purple-100 mt-2">' +
                '<label class="text-[10px] font-black text-purple-600 uppercase tracking-widest mb-4 flex items-center gap-2"><i class="fas fa-bullseye text-purple-500"></i> Objectifs Manuels (Avions/Sem)</label>' +
                '<div class="grid grid-cols-3 sm:grid-cols-4 gap-3 max-h-52 overflow-y-auto pr-2 custom-scrollbar">' + manualWeeksHtml + '</div></div>';
        }

        const theoriqueStyle = isReel ? 'display: none;' : 'display: block;';
        const reelStyle = isReel ? 'display: block;' : 'display: none;';
        const nightStyle = is3x8 ? 'display: block;' : 'display: none;';
        const selectTheo = !isReel ? 'selected' : '';
        const selectReel = isReel ? 'selected' : '';
        const select2x8 = !is3x8 ? 'selected' : '';
        const select3x8 = is3x8 ? 'selected' : '';

        // --- GÉNÉRATION DES CASES À COCHER POUR LA FUSION ---
        let checkboxesHtml = '<div class="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-2 max-h-32 overflow-y-auto hide-scroll p-1 mt-2">';
        if (allWorkstations.length === 0) {
            checkboxesHtml += '<p class="text-[10px] text-sky-600/80 italic col-span-2">Aucun poste configuré dans l\'onglet Général.</p>';
        } else {
            allWorkstations.forEach(ws => {
                const isChecked = includedStationsList.includes(ws) ? 'checked' : '';
                checkboxesHtml += `
                    <label class="flex items-center gap-2 cursor-pointer hover:bg-sky-100/50 p-1.5 rounded-lg transition-colors group">
                        <input type="checkbox" value="${ws}" class="rule-included-station-cb h-3.5 w-3.5 text-[#00b5e2] border-gray-300 rounded focus:ring-[#00b5e2] cursor-pointer" ${isChecked}>
                        <span class="text-[10px] font-bold text-[#00205b] group-hover:text-[#00b5e2] uppercase tracking-widest truncate transition-colors">${ws}</span>
                    </label>
                `;
            });
        }
        checkboxesHtml += '</div>';

        htmlCards += '<div class="capa-rule-card bg-white p-6 rounded-[2rem] border border-gray-100 shadow-sm hover:shadow-[0_10px_30px_rgba(0,32,91,0.08)] transition-all duration-300 relative group overflow-hidden" data-station="' + station + '">' +
            '<div class="absolute left-0 top-0 bottom-0 w-2 bg-orange-400 group-hover:bg-[#00b5e2] transition-colors"></div>' +
            '<div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-6 pl-2">' +
                '<h5 class="font-black text-xl text-[#00205b] uppercase italic tracking-tight">' + station + '</h5>' +
                '<div class="flex gap-2">' +
                    '<select class="rule-mode glass-input bg-indigo-50 border border-indigo-100 text-[11px] font-black text-indigo-800 uppercase tracking-widest rounded-xl px-3 py-2 outline-none cursor-pointer focus:border-[#00b5e2] transition-all shadow-sm" onchange="const card = this.closest(\'.capa-rule-card\'); const isReelVal = this.value === \'reel\'; card.querySelector(\'.mode-theorique\').style.display = isReelVal ? \'none\' : \'block\'; card.querySelector(\'.mode-reel\').style.display = isReelVal ? \'block\' : \'none\';">' +
                        '<option value="theorique" ' + selectTheo + '>Théorique</option>' +
                        '<option value="reel" ' + selectReel + '>Réel</option>' +
                    '</select>' +
                '</div>' +
            '</div>' +
            '<div class="space-y-4 pl-2">' +

                // BLOC DES CASES À COCHER POUR LA FUSION
                '<div class="bg-sky-50/80 p-4 rounded-2xl border border-sky-100 mb-4">' +
                    '<label class="text-[10px] font-black text-sky-700 uppercase tracking-widest flex items-center gap-1.5"><i class="fas fa-object-group"></i> Postes RH Inclus (Fusion)</label>' +
                    checkboxesHtml +
                '</div>' +

                '<div class="mode-theorique space-y-4" style="' + theoriqueStyle + '">' +
                    '<div class="flex justify-between items-end mb-2">' +
                        '<div class="flex flex-col">' +
                            '<label class="text-[9px] font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-widest mb-1 block">TRS (%)</label>' +
                            '<div class="relative">' +
                                '<input type="number" min="0" max="100" class="rule-trs w-20 glass-input bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg pr-5 pl-2 py-1 text-sm font-black text-[#00205b] outline-none focus:border-blue-400 transition-all text-center shadow-sm" value="' + trsValue + '">' +
                                '<span class="absolute right-1.5 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-400">%</span>' +
                            '</div>' +
                        '</div>' +
                        '<select class="rule-cycle glass-input bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 text-[9px] font-black text-[#00205b] uppercase tracking-widest rounded-lg px-2 py-1 outline-none cursor-pointer" onchange="this.closest(\'.capa-rule-card\').querySelector(\'.night-settings\').style.display = this.value === \'3x8\' ? \'block\' : \'none\'">' +
                            '<option value="2x8" ' + select2x8 + '>2x8</option>' +
                            '<option value="3x8" ' + select3x8 + '>3x8</option>' +
                        '</select>' +
                    '</div>' +
                    '<div class="bg-blue-50/60 p-4 rounded-2xl border border-blue-100 mt-2">' +
                        '<h6 class="text-[10px] font-black text-blue-600 uppercase tracking-widest mb-3 flex items-center gap-2"><i class="fas fa-sun text-sm"></i> Équipe Jour</h6>' +
                        '<div class="flex gap-4">' +
                            '<div class="flex-1">' +
                                '<label class="text-[9px] font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-widest mb-1.5 block">Effectif Cible</label>' +
                                '<input type="number" class="rule-staff-day w-full glass-input bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-4 py-2 text-sm font-black text-[#00205b] outline-none focus:border-blue-400 transition-all" value="' + (rule.maxStaffDay || 18) + '">' +
                            '</div>' +
                            '<div class="flex-1">' +
