    if (wsFilterBtn) {
        wsFilterBtn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            e.stopPropagation();
            const opts = document.getElementById('ws-filter-options');
            const chev = document.getElementById('ws-filter-chevron');
            const isHidden = opts.classList.contains('hidden');
            
            window.closeAllDropdowns();
            
            if (isHidden) {
                opts.classList.remove('hidden');
                chev.classList.add('rotate-180');
            }
        });
        // Empêche la fermeture quand on clique DANS le menu
        document.getElementById('ws-filter-options').addEventListener('click', e => e.stopPropagation());
    }

    // --- Écouteurs pour les filtres des listes et la navigation ---
    elements.monthPicker.addEventListener('change', (e) => { state.teamViewDate = e.target.value; fetchAndRenderTeamView(); saveFiltersToLocalStorage(); });
    elements.searchInput.addEventListener('input', (e) => { state.searchQuery = e.target.value; renderPersonnelList(); });
    elements.personnelReapFilter.addEventListener('change', (e) => { state.personnelListReapFilter = e.target.value; renderPersonnelList(); saveFiltersToLocalStorage(); });
    elements.personnelSort.addEventListener('change', (e) => { state.personnelSort = e.target.value; renderPersonnelList(); });

    // Navigation du calendrier annuel (année précédente/suivante)
    document.getElementById('prev-year').addEventListener('click', () => { state.currentYear--; if (state.selectedPersonnelId) selectPersonnel(state.selectedPersonnelId); });
    document.getElementById('next-year').addEventListener('click', () => { state.currentYear++; if (state.selectedPersonnelId) selectPersonnel(state.selectedPersonnelId); });

    // --- Écouteurs pour la VUE INDICATEURS ---
    // Le sélecteur de date recharge TOUTE la vue indicateurs (partie haute et basse)
    elements.indicatorDatePicker.addEventListener('change', () => {
        fetchAndRenderIndicators();
        fetchAndRenderWeeklyComparison();
    });

// --- NOUVEAU FILTRE D'INDICATEURS (DASHBOARD MULTI-CHOIX) ---
    const indicatorFilterButton = document.getElementById('indicator-team-filter-button');
    const indicatorFilterOptions = document.getElementById('indicator-team-filter-options');
    const indicatorFilterChevron = indicatorFilterButton ? indicatorFilterButton.querySelector('.fa-chevron-down') : null;

    if (indicatorFilterButton && indicatorFilterOptions) {
        // Ouverture du menu
        indicatorFilterButton.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            e.stopPropagation();
            const isHidden = indicatorFilterOptions.classList.contains('hidden');
            
            if (typeof window.closeAllDropdowns === 'function') {
                window.closeAllDropdowns();
            }
            
            if (isHidden) {
                indicatorFilterOptions.classList.remove('hidden');
                if (indicatorFilterChevron) indicatorFilterChevron.classList.add('rotate-180');
                populateIndicatorFilter(); 
            }
        });

        // Gestion des cases à cocher (changement de couleur + état) sans fermer le menu
        indicatorFilterOptions.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            e.stopPropagation(); // 🔴 LA CORRECTION EST ICI : On empêche le clic de remonter et de fermer le menu !

            // Si on clique sur le bouton Appliquer (utilisation de closest pour capter aussi l'icône)
            if (e.target.closest('#validate-ind-team-filter-btn')) {
                e.preventDefault();
                indicatorFilterOptions.classList.add('hidden');
                if (indicatorFilterChevron) indicatorFilterChevron.classList.remove('rotate-180');
                
                // On lance le rechargement des graphiques
                fetchAndRenderIndicators();
                fetchAndRenderWeeklyComparison();
                return;
            }

            // Si on clique sur une étiquette (label) contenant une case
            const label = e.target.closest('label');
            if (label) {
                e.preventDefault(); 
                const checkbox = label.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
                if (!checkbox) return;
                
                const clickedValue = checkbox.value;
                let currentSelection = Array.from(indicatorFilterOptions.querySelectorAll('input:checked')).map(cb => cb.value);
                const isCurrentlyChecked = checkbox.checked;
                
                // Logique intelligente des cases à cocher
                if (clickedValue === 'Tous' && !isCurrentlyChecked) {
                    currentSelection = ['Tous'];
                } else if (clickedValue !== 'Tous') {
                    if (!isCurrentlyChecked) {
                        currentSelection.push(clickedValue);
                        currentSelection = currentSelection.filter(val => val !== 'Tous');
                    } else {
                        currentSelection = currentSelection.filter(val => val !== clickedValue);
                    }
                }
                
                if (currentSelection.length === 0) {
                    currentSelection = ['Tous'];
                }
                
                state.indicatorTeamSelection = currentSelection;
                populateIndicatorFilter(); // Redessine le menu pour les couleurs
            }
        });

        // Fermeture de sécurité si on clique ailleurs sur la page
        document.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
            if (!indicatorFilterButton.contains(event.target) && !indicatorFilterOptions.contains(event.target)) {
                indicatorFilterOptions.classList.add('hidden');
                if (indicatorFilterChevron) indicatorFilterChevron.classList.remove('rotate-180');
            }
        });
    }

    // --- Écouteur pour le filtre de quart de travail (NOUVEAU) ---
    document.getElementById('shift-filter-buttons').addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        const button = e.target.closest('button');
        if (!button) return;

        const newShift = button.getAttribute('data-shift');
        
        // Si l'utilisateur clique sur le bouton déjà sélectionné, on ne fait rien
        if (button.getAttribute('aria-selected') === 'true' && newShift !== 'null') return;
        
        // Mise à jour de l'état
        state.shiftFilter = (newShift === 'null') ? null : newShift;

        // Mise à jour de l'affichage
        document.querySelectorAll('#shift-filter-buttons button').forEach(btn => {
             btn.setAttribute('aria-selected', btn.getAttribute('data-shift') === newShift);
        });

        // On recharge la vue d'équipe avec le nouveau filtre
        fetchAndRenderTeamView();
    });
    // --- FIN ÉCOUTEUR FILTRE QUART ---

    // --- Écouteurs pour la modale des paramètres ---

// Logique des onglets (CORRIGÉE POUR FLEXBOX)
    document.getElementById('settings-tabs').addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        const tabButton = e.target.closest('.settings-tab-btn');
        if (tabButton) {
            const tab = tabButton.dataset.tab;

            // Met à jour les boutons
            document.querySelectorAll('.settings-tab-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.classList.remove('is-active');
            });
            tabButton.classList.add('is-active');

            // Met à jour les panneaux de contenu
            document.querySelectorAll('.settings-tab-content').forEach(content => {
                content.classList.add('hidden');
                content.classList.remove('flex'); // Assure qu'il n'y a pas de conflit
            });
            
            const targetContent = document.getElementById(`tab-content-${tab}`);
            targetContent.classList.remove('hidden');
            targetContent.classList.add('flex'); // Indispensable pour la structure interne
        }
    });

    // Clic sur les boutons
    document.getElementById('settings-modal-close').addEventListener('click', closeSettingsModal);
    document.getElementById('settings-modal-cancel-general').addEventListener('click', closeSettingsModal);
    document.getElementById('settings-modal-cancel-access').addEventListener('click', closeSettingsModal);
    document.getElementById('save-settings-general-btn').addEventListener('click', handleSaveGeneralSettings);
    document.getElementById('save-settings-access-btn').addEventListener('click', handleSaveAccessSettings);
    document.getElementById('add-role-btn').addEventListener('click', addRoleToSettingsList);
    document.getElementById('add-role-assignment-btn').addEventListener('click', addRoleAssignmentToUI);

    document.getElementById('generate-next-year-btn').addEventListener('click', handleGenerateNextYear);
    document.getElementById('archive-previous-year-btn').addEventListener('click', handleArchivePreviousYear);

    // Ajout avec la touche "Entrée"
    document.getElementById('setting-new-role').addEventListener('keydown', (e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter') { e.preventDefault(); addRoleToSettingsList(); }});
    document.getElementById('setting-new-user-email').addEventListener('keydown', (e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter') { e.preventDefault(); addRoleAssignmentToUI(); }});

    // Fermeture de la modale en cliquant sur le fond
    document.getElementById('settings-modal').addEventListener('click', (event) => {
        if (event.target === event.currentTarget) {
            closeSettingsModal();
        }
    });

    document.getElementById('settings-modal-cancel-capa').addEventListener('click', closeSettingsModal);
    
document.getElementById('save-settings-capa-btn').addEventListener('click', async function() {
    const btn = this;
    const originalText = btn.innerHTML;
    
    // 1. Griser le bouton
    btn.disabled = true;
    btn.classList.add('opacity-50', 'cursor-not-allowed');
    btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin text-lg"></i> <span>Enregistrement...</span>';
    
    // 2. Fermer la modale instantanément et afficher le loader de fond
    closeSettingsModal();
    showLoader(true);
    
    try {
        const selectedStations = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.capa-station-cb:checked')).map(cb => cb.value);
        const targetModeSelect = document.getElementById('setting-target-mode');
        const targetMode = targetModeSelect ? targetModeSelect.value : (state.settings.targetMode || 'auto');
        
        const newManualTargets = {};
        const newCapaRules = {};

        document.querySelectorAll('.capa-rule-card').forEach(card => {
            const station = card.dataset.station;
            
            // --- LECTURE DES CASES À COCHER POUR LA FUSION ---
            const checkedIncludedBoxes = Array.from(card.querySelectorAll('.rule-included-station-cb:checked')).map(cb => cb.value);
            // Si aucune case n'est cochée, on prend le nom du poste par défaut
            const includedStationsVal = checkedIncludedBoxes.length > 0 ? checkedIncludedBoxes.join(',') : station;
            
            const manualInputs = card.querySelectorAll('.rule-manual-target-week');
            if (manualInputs.length > 0) {
                newManualTargets[station] = {};
                manualInputs.forEach(input => {
                    const w = input.dataset.week;
                    newManualTargets[station][w] = parseFloat(input.value) || 0;
                });
            }

            const mappingSelect = card.querySelector('.rule-mapping');
            const mappingValue = mappingSelect ? mappingSelect.value : '';

            newCapaRules[station] = {
                includedStations: includedStationsVal, // 🔴 C'est ici qu'on enregistre les cases cochées
                calcMode: card.querySelector('.rule-mode').value,
                cycle: card.querySelector('.rule-cycle').value,
                trs: parseFloat(card.querySelector('.rule-trs').value) || 100,
                maxStaffDay: parseFloat(card.querySelector('.rule-staff-day').value),
                maxCapDay: parseFloat(card.querySelector('.rule-cap-day').value),
                maxStaffNight: parseFloat(card.querySelector('.rule-staff-night') ? card.querySelector('.rule-staff-night').value : 9) || 9,
                maxCapNight: parseFloat(card.querySelector('.rule-cap-night') ? card.querySelector('.rule-cap-night').value : 1.2) || 1.2,
                prodTime: parseFloat(card.querySelector('.rule-prod-time') ? card.querySelector('.rule-prod-time').value : 10) || 10,
                mapping: mappingValue
            };
        });

        const newConfig = {
            ...state.settings,
            targetMode: targetMode,
            manualTargets: newManualTargets,
            capaWorkstations: selectedStations,
            capaRules: newCapaRules
        };

        await serverCall('saveConfiguration', [newConfig]);
        state.settings = newConfig;
        
        showToast("Paramètres CAPA enregistrés.", false);
        
        // Rafraîchir les données pour que le tableau de bord utilise la nouvelle fusion
        loadCapaData();

    } catch (e) {
        showToast(`Erreur : ${e.message}`, true);
    } finally {
        btn.disabled = false;
        btn.classList.remove('opacity-50', 'cursor-not-allowed');
        btn.innerHTML = originalText;
    }
});

    // --- Écouteurs pour les autres actions (impression, modales, etc.) ---
    elements.printTeamScheduleBtn.addEventListener('click', handlePrintTeamSchedule);

    document.getElementById('mass-update-btn').addEventListener('click', openMassUpdateModal);
    document.getElementById('mass-update-cancel').addEventListener('click', closeMassUpdateModal);
    document.getElementById('mass-update-submit').addEventListener('click', handleMassUpdateSubmit);
    document.getElementById('mass-update-modal').addEventListener('click', (e) => { if (e.target === e.currentTarget) closeMassUpdateModal(); });

    document.getElementById('indicator-modal-close').addEventListener('click', closeIndicatorModal);
    document.getElementById('indicator-modal').addEventListener('click', (e) => { if (e.target === e.currentTarget) closeIndicatorModal(); });

// --- Écouteur pour le filtre de la VUE ÉQUIPE ---
    elements.teamViewFilterButton.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.stopPropagation();
        const isHidden = elements.teamViewFilterContainer.classList.contains('hidden');
        
        window.closeAllDropdowns(); // On ferme tout le reste
        
        if (isHidden) {
            elements.teamViewFilterContainer.classList.remove('hidden');
            const chevron = elements.teamViewFilterButton.querySelector('.fa-chevron-down');
            if (chevron) chevron.classList.add('rotate-180');
            setupTeamFilter();
        }
    });

    // Gère le changement des cases à cocher SANS recharger les données
    elements.teamViewFilterContainer.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
        if (e.target.type === 'checkbox') {
            const clickedValue = e.target.value;
            let currentSelection = Array.from(elements.teamViewFilterContainer.querySelectorAll('input:checked')).map(cb => cb.value);

            if (clickedValue === 'Tous' && e.target.checked) {
                currentSelection = ['Tous'];
            } else if (clickedValue !== 'Tous' && e.target.checked) {
                currentSelection = currentSelection.filter(val => val !== 'Tous');
            }

            // On retire la logique de sélection RP unique ici car elle ne semble pas coller aux exigences de fusion.
            // On conserve plutôt l'état actuel pour permettre la multi-sélection REAP.
            
            if (currentSelection.length === 0) {
                currentSelection = ['Tous'];
            }

            state.teamViewSelection = currentSelection;
            // On redessine le filtre pour mettre à jour l'état visuel des cases (ex: décocher "Tous")
            // et pour afficher/masquer le filtre de quart.
            setupTeamFilter();
        }
    });

    // Gère le clic sur le bouton "Appliquer"
    elements.teamViewFilterContainer.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        // On vérifie si l'élément cliqué est bien notre bouton
        if (e.target.id === 'validate-team-filter-btn') {
            e.preventDefault(); // Empêche le comportement par défaut

            // C'est seulement ici qu'on lance le rechargement et la sauvegarde
            fetchAndRenderTeamView();
            saveFiltersToLocalStorage();
            elements.teamViewFilterContainer.classList.add('hidden'); // On ferme la liste
        }
    });

// --- Écouteurs globaux pour fermer les pop-ups ---
    document.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
        // 1. Pour le sélecteur de statut
        if (!elements.statusSelector.classList.contains('hidden') && !elements.statusSelector.contains(event.target) && !event.target.closest('.calendar-day-wrapper, .team-view-cell-wrapper')) {
            closeEditor();
        }
        
        // 2. Pour le filtre des équipes (REAP)
        if (!elements.teamViewFilterButton.contains(event.target) && !elements.teamViewFilterContainer.contains(event.target)) {
            elements.teamViewFilterContainer.classList.add('hidden');
            const teamChevron = elements.teamViewFilterButton.querySelector('.fa-chevron-down');
            if (teamChevron) teamChevron.classList.remove('rotate-180');
        }

        // 3. NOUVEAU : Pour le filtre par Poste
        const wsFilterBtn = document.getElementById('ws-filter-button');
        const wsFilterOpts = document.getElementById('ws-filter-options');
        const wsChevron = document.getElementById('ws-filter-chevron');
        
        if (wsFilterOpts && !wsFilterOpts.classList.contains('hidden')) {
            if (!wsFilterBtn.contains(event.target) && !wsFilterOpts.contains(event.target)) {
                wsFilterOpts.classList.add('hidden');
                if (wsChevron) wsChevron.classList.remove('rotate-180');
            }
        }
    });
});

// =========================================================
// === MODULE CHARGE CAPA (Palette Solaire & Réel) ===
// =========================================================

let capaCharts = {};
let mainCapaChart = null;
let currentCapaViewMode = '10w'; // NOUVEAU : Mode par défaut sur 10 semaines

// NOUVEAU : Fonction pour basculer l'affichage
window.setCapaViewMode = function(mode) {
    currentCapaViewMode = mode;
    const btn10w = document.getElementById('capa-view-10w');
    const btnYear = document.getElementById('capa-view-year');
    
    // Nouvelles classes avec la bonne hauteur (h-full) et le style bleu nuit/blanc
    const activeClass = "flex-1 sm:flex-none h-full px-5 rounded-lg text-[11px] font-black uppercase tracking-wider transition-all bg-[#00205b] text-white shadow-sm";
    const inactiveClass = "flex-1 sm:flex-none h-full px-5 rounded-lg text-[11px] font-black uppercase tracking-wider transition-all text-gray-400 hover:text-[#00205b] bg-transparent";

    if (mode === '10w') {
        btn10w.className = activeClass;
        btnYear.className = inactiveClass;
    } else {
        btnYear.className = activeClass;
        btn10w.className = inactiveClass;
    }

    // Rafraîchit le graphique automatiquement sur le poste actuellement sélectionné
    const stationNameEl = document.getElementById('station-name-span');
    if (stationNameEl && stationNameEl.textContent !== '...' && window.currentSwitchStation) {
        window.currentSwitchStation(stationNameEl.textContent);
    }
};

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    const savedYear = localStorage.getItem('capa_dashboard_year');
    const yearSelect = document.getElementById('capa-year-select');
    if (savedYear && yearSelect) {
        yearSelect.value = savedYear;
    }
});

async function loadCapaData() {
    const yearSelect = document.getElementById('capa-year-select');
    if (!yearSelect) return;
    
    const year = yearSelect.value;
    localStorage.setItem('capa_dashboard_year', year);

    showLoader(true);
    try {
        const data = await serverCall('getCapaDashboardData', [parseInt(year)]);
        // Sécurité si l'erreur vient du backend
        if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
        renderCapaDashboard(data);
    } catch (e) {
        showToast("Erreur chargement Capa : " + e.message, true);
    } finally {
        hideLoader();
    }
}

// Fonction pour sauvegarder la saisie du Réel
window.handleSaveReel = async () => {
    const station = document.getElementById('station-name-span').textContent;
    const week = document.getElementById('reel-week-select').value;
    const val = document.getElementById('reel-value-input').value;
    const year = document.getElementById('capa-year-select').value;
    
    showLoader(true);
    try {
        await serverCall('saveCapaReel', [year, week, station, val]);
        showToast("Production réelle enregistrée", false);
        await loadCapaData(); // On rafraîchit le graphique
    } catch(e) {
        showToast("Erreur : " + e.message, true);
    } finally {
        hideLoader();
    }
};

function renderCapaDashboard(data) {
    const container = document.getElementById('capa-charts-container');
    if (!container) return;
    container.innerHTML = ''; 

    Object.values(capaCharts).forEach(chart => chart.destroy());
    capaCharts = {};

    if (!data || Object.keys(data).length === 0) {
        container.innerHTML = `<div class="glass p-10 text-center text-[#00205b] font-black uppercase tracking-widest border-2 border-white rounded-[2rem] shadow-xl">${t('capa_no_data')}</div>`;
        return;
    }

    const THEORETICAL_CAPS = {
        '2x8': { 'Matin': 10.5, 'Après-Midi': 8.4, 'Nuit': 0 },
        '3x8': { 'Matin': 7.5, 'Après-Midi': 7.5, 'Nuit': 4.8 }
    };

    const sortedStations = state.settings.capaWorkstations && state.settings.capaWorkstations.length > 0 
                   ? state.settings.capaWorkstations 
                   : Object.keys(data); 
   
    const chartWrapper = document.createElement('div');
    chartWrapper.className = "glass bg-white p-8 rounded-[2.5rem] shadow-2xl border-2 border-white relative h-[650px] flex flex-col overflow-hidden";
    
    let weekOptions = '';
    for(let i=1; i<=52; i++) weekOptions += `<option value="${i}">S${i}</option>`;

    const legendHtml = `
        <div class="flex flex-wrap justify-center items-center gap-3 md:gap-4 mb-6 text-[10px] font-black text-[#00205b] uppercase tracking-widest">
            <div class="flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl border border-gray-200 shadow-sm"><span class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full block" style="background-color:#60A5FA;"></span> ${t('shift_m')}</div>
            <div class="flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl border border-gray-200 shadow-sm"><span class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full block" style="background-color:#FBBF24;"></span> ${t('shift_a')}</div>
            <div class="flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl border border-gray-200 shadow-sm"><span class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full block" style="background-color:#312E81;"></span> ${t('shift_n')}</div>
            <div class="flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl border border-gray-200 shadow-sm"><span class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full block" style="background-color:#10B981;"></span> ${t('capa_legend_ot')}</div>
            <div class="flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl border border-gray-200 shadow-sm"><span class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full block border" style="background-color:rgba(248,113,113,0.4); border-color:#F87171;"></span> ${t('capa_legend_deficit')}</div>
            <div class="flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl border border-gray-200 shadow-sm"><span class="w-5 h-1 block rounded-full" style="background-color:#EF4444;"></span> ${t('capa_legend_target')}</div>
            <div class="flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl border border-gray-200 shadow-sm"><span class="w-5 h-1 block rounded-full" style="background-color:#8B5CF6;"></span> ${t('capa_legend_real')}</div>
        </div>
    `;
    
chartWrapper.innerHTML = `
        <div class="absolute -left-10 -top-10 w-64 h-64 bg-[#00b5e2]/10 rounded-full blur-3xl pointer-events-none z-0"></div>
        
        <div class="relative z-50 flex flex-col lg:flex-row justify-between items-start lg:items-center border-b border-gray-100/60 pb-5 mb-5 gap-6">
             <div>
                  <h3 class="text-2xl font-black text-[#00205b] uppercase tracking-tighter italic flex items-center gap-3">
                       <div class="w-10 h-10 bg-[#00205b] text-white rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center shadow-md rotate-3 shrink-0"><i class="fas fa-chart-line text-lg"></i></div>
                       <span>${t('capa_analysis')}</span> <span id="main-chart-title" class="text-[#00b5e2]">...</span>
                  </h3>
             </div>
             
             <div class="flex flex-col md:flex-row items-center gap-4 w-full lg:w-auto">
                  
                  <div class="relative z-30 w-full md:w-auto" id="station-dropdown-wrapper">
                      <button id="station-dropdown-btn" class="glass-input flex items-center justify-between w-full md:w-72 h-[48px] bg-white border-2 border-transparent hover:border-[#00b5e2]/30 rounded-2xl px-4 shadow-sm hover:shadow-md transition-all duration-300 group" onclick="document.getElementById('station-dropdown-menu').classList.toggle('hidden'); document.getElementById('station-dropdown-chevron').classList.toggle('rotate-180'); event.stopPropagation();">
                          <div class="flex items-center truncate gap-3">
                              <div class="w-8 h-8 rounded-xl bg-[#00205b]/5 text-[#00205b] flex items-center justify-center group-hover:bg-[#00b5e2] group-hover:text-white transition-colors shrink-0">
                                  <i class="fas fa-layer-group text-sm"></i>
                              </div>
                              <span id="station-name-span" class="text-[12px] font-black text-[#00205b] uppercase tracking-widest truncate mt-0.5">...</span>
                          </div>
                          <div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-full bg-gray-50 flex items-center justify-center group-hover:bg-[#00b5e2]/10 transition-colors shrink-0">
                              <i id="station-dropdown-chevron" class="fas fa-chevron-down text-gray-400 group-hover:text-[#00b5e2] text-[10px] transition-transform duration-300"></i>
                          </div>
                      </button>

                      <div id="station-dropdown-menu" class="absolute top-[calc(100%+8px)] right-0 md:left-0 w-full md:w-72 max-h-[300px] overflow-y-auto hide-scroll rounded-2xl bg-white/95 backdrop-blur-xl p-2 shadow-[0_15px_40px_-5px_rgba(0,32,91,0.2)] hidden border border-white flex flex-col z-[60]">
                          </div>
                  </div>

                  <div class="flex items-center gap-2 bg-purple-50 p-2 rounded-2xl border border-purple-100 shadow-sm shrink-0 w-full md:w-auto">
                       <span class="text-[10px] font-black text-purple-800 uppercase tracking-widest pl-2 flex items-center gap-1.5"><i class="fas fa-edit"></i> ${t('capa_enter_real')}</span>
                       <select id="reel-week-select" class="glass-input h-9 px-2 text-[10px] font-black text-[#00205b] w-16 uppercase bg-white cursor-pointer rounded-lg border-transparent focus:border-purple-300 outline-none">${weekOptions}</select>
                       <input type="number" step="0.5" id="reel-value-input" placeholder="${t('capa_qty')}" class="glass-input h-9 w-16 px-2 text-xs font-bold text-[#00205b] text-center bg-white outline-none rounded-lg border-transparent focus:border-purple-300">
                       <button onclick="handleSaveReel()" class="w-9 h-9 bg-purple-600 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-purple-500 transition-colors flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm hover:shadow-md active:scale-95"><i class="fas fa-check"></i></button>
                  </div>
             </div>
        </div>
        <div class="relative z-10">${legendHtml}</div>
        <div class="flex-grow relative z-10 w-full"><canvas id="main-capa-chart"></canvas></div>
    `;

    container.appendChild(chartWrapper);
    const dropdownMenu = document.getElementById('station-dropdown-menu');

    // KPIs Globaux
    let totalWeeks = 0, criticalWeeks = 0, okWeeks = 0, totalCoverageSum = 0;
    sortedStations.forEach(station => {
        const sData = data[station];
        if (!sData) return;
        sData.data.forEach(d => {
            totalWeeks++;
            totalCoverageSum += d.coverage;
            if (d.status === 'sous-capacite') criticalWeeks++; else okWeeks++;
        });
    });
    
    const globalAvg = totalWeeks > 0 ? (totalCoverageSum / totalWeeks) : 0;
    const validStationsCount = sortedStations.filter(s => data[s]).length;
    let avgCritical = 0; let avgOk = 0;
    if (validStationsCount > 0) {
        avgCritical = Math.round(criticalWeeks / validStationsCount);
        avgOk = 52 - avgCritical; 
    }
    
    if(document.getElementById('kpi-capa-coverage')) {
        document.getElementById('kpi-capa-coverage').textContent = `${globalAvg.toFixed(0)}%`;
    }
    if(document.getElementById('kpi-capa-risk')) {
        document.getElementById('kpi-capa-risk').textContent = avgCritical;
    }
    if(document.getElementById('kpi-capa-ok')) {
        document.getElementById('kpi-capa-ok').textContent = avgOk;
    }
    
    const switchStation = (stationName) => {
        window.currentSwitchStation = switchStation; 
        
        // Mise à jour des titres (le dropdown + le gros titre)
        document.getElementById('station-name-span').textContent = stationName;
        document.getElementById('main-chart-title').textContent = stationName;

        const stationData = data[stationName];
        if (!stationData) return;

        let weeks = stationData.weeks;
        let rawData = stationData.data;

        // --- FILTRAGE SELON LA VUE (10 SEMAINES OU ANNEE) ---
        if (currentCapaViewMode === '10w') {
            const selectedYear = parseInt(document.getElementById('capa-year-select').value) || new Date().getFullYear();
            const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
            
            // Fonction rapide pour trouver le numéro de semaine ISO actuel
            const getISOWeek = (date) => {
                const d = new Date(Date.UTC(date.getFullYear(), date.getMonth(), date.getDate()));
                const dayNum = d.getUTCDay() || 7;
                d.setUTCDate(d.getUTCDate() + 4 - dayNum);
                const yearStart = new Date(Date.UTC(d.getUTCFullYear(),0,1));
                return Math.ceil((((d - yearStart) / 86400000) + 1)/7);
            };
            
            let startWeek = 1;
            if (selectedYear === currentYear) {
                startWeek = getISOWeek(new Date()); 
            } else if (selectedYear < currentYear) {
                startWeek = 43; 
            }

            // Découpage : on garde 10 semaines (actuelle + 9 suivantes)
            const startIndex = Math.max(0, startWeek - 1);
            const endIndex = Math.min(startIndex + 10, 52); 

            weeks = weeks.slice(startIndex, endIndex);
            rawData = rawData.slice(startIndex, endIndex);
        }
        // --------------------------------------------------------------

        const targets = rawData.map(d => d.target);
        const dataReel = rawData.map(d => d.reel);
        const dataM = rawData.map(d => d.breakdown.M);
        const dataA = rawData.map(d => d.breakdown.A);
        const dataN = rawData.map(d => d.breakdown.N);
        const dataHS = rawData.map(d => d.breakdown.HS);
        const dataGap = rawData.map(d => {
            const deficit = d.target - d.realCapacity;
            return deficit > 0 ? deficit : 0;
        });

        if (mainCapaChart) mainCapaChart.destroy();
        const ctx = document.getElementById('main-capa-chart').getContext('2d');
        
        mainCapaChart = new Chart(ctx, {
            type: 'bar',
            data: {
                labels: weeks,
                datasets: [
                    { 
                        label: t('capa_legend_real'), 
                        data: dataReel, 
                        type: 'line', 
                        borderColor: '#8B5CF6', 
                        borderWidth: 3, 
                        pointRadius: 4, 
                        pointBackgroundColor: '#ffffff',
                        pointBorderColor: '#8B5CF6',
                        pointHoverRadius: 7,
                        tension: 0.2, 
                        stack: 'ReelStack', 
                        order: 0, 
                        zIndex: 11,
                        spanGaps: true 
                    },
                    { 
                        label: t('capa_legend_target'), 
                        data: targets, 
                        type: 'line', 
                        borderColor: '#EF4444', 
                        borderWidth: 3, 
                        pointRadius: 0, 
                        pointHoverRadius: 5,
                        tension: 0, 
                        stack: 'ObjStack', 
                        order: 1, 
                        zIndex: 10 
                    },
                    { 
                        label: t('shift_m'), 
                        data: dataM, 
                        backgroundColor: '#60A5FA',
                        stack: 'Stack 0',
                        order: 2,
                        borderRadius: { bottomLeft: 4, bottomRight: 4 }
                    },
                    { 
                        label: t('shift_a'), 
                        data: dataA, 
                        backgroundColor: '#FBBF24',
                        stack: 'Stack 0',
                        order: 3
                    },
                    { 
                        label: t('shift_n'), 
                        data: dataN, 
                        backgroundColor: '#312E81',
                        stack: 'Stack 0',
                        order: 4
                    },
                    { 
                        label: t('capa_legend_ot'), 
                        data: dataHS, 
                        backgroundColor: '#10B981',
                        stack: 'Stack 0',
                        order: 5,
                        datalabels: {
                            display: function(context) { return Math.abs(context.dataset.data[context.dataIndex]) > 0.1; },
                            color: 'white',
                            font: { weight: 'bold', size: 10 },
                            formatter: (val) => val > 0 ? "+" + Math.round(val) : Math.round(val)
                        }
                    },
                    { 
                        label: t('capa_legend_deficit'), 
                        data: dataGap, 
                        backgroundColor: 'rgba(248, 113, 113, 0.4)',
                        borderColor: '#F87171', 
                        borderWidth: 1,
                        borderDash: [4, 4],
                        stack: 'Stack 0', 
                        order: 6,
                        borderRadius: { topLeft: 6, topRight: 6 },
                        datalabels: { display: false }
                    }
                ]
            },
            options: {
                responsive: true, 
                maintainAspectRatio: false, 
                animation: { duration: 400 },
                interaction: { mode: 'index', intersect: false },
                plugins: { 
                    title: { display: false },
                    legend: { display: false }, 
                    datalabels: { display: false },
                    tooltip: { 
                        backgroundColor: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.98)',
                        titleColor: '#00205b',
                        bodyColor: '#374151',
                        borderColor: '#e2e8f0',
                        borderWidth: 1,
                        padding: 16, 
                        boxPadding: 8,
                        cornerRadius: 12,
                        boxShadow: '0 10px 25px -5px rgba(0, 32, 91, 0.1)',
                        callbacks: {
                            title: function(tooltipItems) {
                                return tooltipItems[0].label;
                            },
                            label: function() { return null; },
                            afterBody: (tooltipItems) => {
                                const idx = tooltipItems[0].dataIndex;
                                const d = rawData[idx];
                                const rule = d.rule || {};
                                const isReel = rule.calcMode === 'reel';

                                const gap = d.realCapacity - d.target;
                                const deficitText = gap < 0 
                                    ? `${t('capa_tt_deficit')} ${Math.abs(gap).toFixed(1)}${t('capa_tt_planes')}` 
                                    : `${t('capa_tt_excess')}${gap.toFixed(1)}${t('capa_tt_planes')}`;
                                
                                const hsSign = d.breakdown.HS > 0 ? '+' : '';
                                const realText = d.reel !== null 
                                    ? `${t('capa_tt_real_prod')} ${d.reel}${t('capa_tt_planes')}` 
                                    : `${t('capa_tt_real_prod')} -`;

                                let lines = [
                                    `${t('capa_tt_target')} ${d.target.toFixed(1)}${t('capa_tt_planes')}`,
                                    realText,
                                    `----------------------------------`
                                ];
                                
                                if (isReel) {
                                    lines.push(`${t('capa_tt_realtime_base')}${rule.prodTime || 10}h) :`);
                                    lines.push(`${t('capa_tt_morning')} ${d.staffBreakdown.M.toFixed(1)}${t('capa_tt_etp')}`);
                                    lines.push(`${t('capa_tt_afternoon')} ${d.staffBreakdown.A.toFixed(1)}${t('capa_tt_etp')}`);
                                    if (d.teamCount === 3) {
                                        lines.push(`${t('capa_tt_night')} ${d.staffBreakdown.N.toFixed(1)}${t('capa_tt_etp')}`);
                                    }
                                } else {
                                    const targetDay = rule.maxStaffDay || 18;
                                    const targetNight = rule.maxStaffNight || 9;
                                    lines.push(`${t('capa_tt_staff_vs_target')}`);
                                    lines.push(`${t('capa_tt_morning')} ${d.staffBreakdown.M.toFixed(1)}${t('capa_tt_pers')} ${targetDay})`);
                                    lines.push(`${t('capa_tt_afternoon')} ${d.staffBreakdown.A.toFixed(1)}${t('capa_tt_pers')} ${targetDay})`);
                                    if (d.teamCount === 3) {
                                        lines.push(`${t('capa_tt_night')} ${d.staffBreakdown.N.toFixed(1)}${t('capa_tt_pers')} ${targetNight})`);
                                    }
                                }

                                lines = lines.concat([
                                    `----------------------------------`,
                                    `${t('capa_tt_ot_hours')} ${d.hsHours.toFixed(1)}${t('capa_tt_hours')}`,
                                    `${t('capa_tt_capa_gained')} ${hsSign}${d.breakdown.HS.toFixed(1)}${t('capa_tt_planes')}`,
                                    `----------------------------------`,
                                    `${t('capa_tt_total_est')} ${d.realCapacity.toFixed(1)}${t('capa_tt_planes')}`,
                                    `${t('capa_tt_coverage')} ${d.coverage.toFixed(0)}%`,
                                    ``,
                                    deficitText
                                ]);

                                return lines;
                            }
                        }
                    } 
                },
                scales: { 
                    y: { 
                        stacked: true, 
                        beginAtZero: true, 
                        title: { display: true, text: t('capa_y_axis') || 'Avions / Semaine', font: { weight: 'bold', family: "'Inter', sans-serif" } }, 
                        grid: { color: '#f1f5f9' },
                        ticks: { font: { weight: 'bold' } }
                    }, 
                    x: { 
                        stacked: true, 
                        grid: { display: false }, 
                        ticks: { maxTicksLimit: 20, font: { weight: 'bold', size: 10 } } 
                    } 
                }
            }
        });
    };

    // --- CRÉATION DES OPTIONS DU MENU DÉROULANT ---
    sortedStations.forEach(station => {
        if (data[station]) {
            const optionBtn = document.createElement('button');
            optionBtn.className = "flex items-center w-full px-4 py-3 cursor-pointer rounded-xl hover:bg-gray-50 transition-colors mb-1 group text-left";
            
            optionBtn.innerHTML = `
                <div class="w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-gray-300 group-hover:bg-[#00b5e2] transition-colors mr-3 station-dot shrink-0"></div>
                <span class="text-[11px] font-black text-[#00205b] uppercase tracking-widest group-hover:text-[#00b5e2] transition-colors truncate mt-0.5">${station}</span>
            `;

            optionBtn.onclick = (e) => {
                e.stopPropagation();
                
                // Mettre en surbrillance l'option sélectionnée
                document.querySelectorAll('#station-dropdown-menu button').forEach(b => {
                    b.classList.remove('bg-blue-50/50');
                    b.querySelector('.station-dot').classList.replace('bg-[#00b5e2]', 'bg-gray-300');
                });
                optionBtn.classList.add('bg-blue-50/50');
                optionBtn.querySelector('.station-dot').classList.replace('bg-gray-300', 'bg-[#00b5e2]');

                // Fermer le menu
                dropdownMenu.classList.add('hidden');
                document.getElementById('station-dropdown-chevron').classList.remove('rotate-180');
                
                // Mettre à jour le graphique
                switchStation(station);
            };

            dropdownMenu.appendChild(optionBtn);
        }
    });

    // Écouteur global pour fermer le menu si clic en dehors
    document.removeEventListener('click', window._capaDropdownListener);
    window._capaDropdownListener = (e) => {
        const btn = document.getElementById('station-dropdown-btn');
        const menu = document.getElementById('station-dropdown-menu');
        if (btn && menu && !btn.contains(e.target) && !menu.contains(e.target)) {
            menu.classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('station-dropdown-chevron').classList.remove('rotate-180');
        }
    };
    document.addEventListener('click', window._capaDropdownListener);

    // Initialisation sur le premier poste valide
    const firstValidStation = sortedStations.find(s => data[s]);
    if (firstValidStation) {
        // Simuler le clic sur la première option pour activer les bons styles
        const firstOption = dropdownMenu.querySelector('button');
        if (firstOption) firstOption.click();
        else switchStation(firstValidStation);
    } else {
         container.innerHTML += `<div class="text-center text-red-500 font-bold mt-4">${t('capa_no_data')}</div>`;
    }
}

    /**
     * [FONCTION DE NAVIGATION UNIFIÉE]
     * Remplace l'ancienne fonction switchView pour gérer les 4 vues correctement.
     */
    function switchView(viewName) {
        // 1. Fermer les éventuelles popups (statut, filtres)
        closeEditor();
        if(elements && elements.teamViewFilterContainer) elements.teamViewFilterContainer.classList.add('hidden');
        if(document.getElementById('indicator-team-filter-options')) document.getElementById('indicator-team-filter-options').classList.add('hidden');

        // 2. Définition des correspondances (Nom Vue -> ID DOM)
        // Attention : les IDs doivent correspondre exactement à votre HTML
        const viewsMap = {
            'individuelle': { id: 'vue-individuelle', btn: 'btn-vue-individuelle' },
            'equipe':       { id: 'vue-equipe',       btn: 'btn-vue-equipe' },
            'indicateurs':  { id: 'vue-indicateurs',  btn: 'btn-vue-indicateurs' },
            'capa':         { id: 'vue-capa',         btn: 'btn-vue-capa' }
        };

        // 3. On masque TOUTES les vues et on désactive TOUS les boutons
        Object.values(viewsMap).forEach(config => {
            const el = document.getElementById(config.id);
            const btn = document.getElementById(config.btn);
            
            if (el) {
                el.classList.add('hidden'); // Utilisation stricte de la classe Tailwind
                el.style.display = '';      // Nettoyage des styles inline qui bloquent
            }
            if (btn) {
                btn.setAttribute('aria-selected', 'false');
            }
        });

        // 4. On active la vue demandée
        const target = viewsMap[viewName];
        if (target) {
            const el = document.getElementById(target.id);
            const btn = document.getElementById(target.btn);

            if (el) el.classList.remove('hidden');
            if (btn) btn.setAttribute('aria-selected', 'true');

            // 5. Chargement des données spécifiques si nécessaire
            if (viewName === 'equipe' && Object.keys(state.teamPresences).length === 0) {
                fetchAndRenderTeamView();
            }
            if (viewName === 'indicateurs') {
                if (!state.indicatorData) fetchAndRenderIndicators();
                fetchAndRenderWeeklyComparison();
            }
            if (viewName === 'capa') {
                // On charge les données Capa seulement quand on clique sur l'onglet
                loadCapaData();
            }
        } else {
            console.error("Vue inconnue : " + viewName);
        }
    }

/**
 * Filtre la liste des postes CAPA dans les paramètres selon la recherche
 */
window.filterCapaStations = function() {
    const query = document.getElementById('capa-station-search').value.toLowerCase().trim();
    const stationsLabels = document.querySelectorAll('#capa-stations-list label');
    let visibleCount = 0;
    
    stationsLabels.forEach(label => {
        const stationName = label.querySelector('span').textContent.toLowerCase();
        if (stationName.includes(query)) {
            // CORRECTION ICI : On vide le style inline au lieu de forcer 'flex'
            // Cela permet à la carte de reprendre sa largeur 100% de la grille
            label.style.display = ''; 
            visibleCount++;
        } else {
            label.style.display = 'none';
        }
    });

    // Affiche un message si aucun poste n'est trouvé
    let noResultMsg = document.getElementById('capa-no-result-msg');
    if (visibleCount === 0 && stationsLabels.length > 0) {
        if (!noResultMsg) {
            noResultMsg = document.createElement('p');
            noResultMsg.id = 'capa-no-result-msg';
            noResultMsg.className = 'text-xs text-red-500 font-bold col-span-full mt-2 text-center bg-red-50 py-2 rounded-xl border border-red-100';
            noResultMsg.textContent = 'Aucun poste ne correspond à votre recherche.';
            document.getElementById('capa-stations-list').appendChild(noResultMsg);
        } else {
            noResultMsg.style.display = 'block';
        }
    } else if (noResultMsg) {
        noResultMsg.style.display = 'none';
    }
};

/**
 * Affiche la modale de doublon et attend le choix de l'utilisateur.
 * @returns {Promise<boolean>} True si on force l'ajout, False si on annule.
 */
function askDuplicateConfirmation(messageHtml) {
    return new Promise((resolve) => {
        const modal = document.getElementById('duplicate-warning-modal');
        const textEl = document.getElementById('duplicate-warning-text');
        const btnCancel = document.getElementById('btn-cancel-duplicate');
        const btnForce = document.getElementById('btn-force-duplicate');

        textEl.innerHTML = messageHtml;
        modal.classList.remove('hidden');

        // Nettoyage des événements pour éviter les clics multiples
        const cleanup = () => {
            btnCancel.removeEventListener('click', onCancel);
            btnForce.removeEventListener('click', onForce);
            modal.classList.add('hidden');
        };

        const onCancel = () => { cleanup(); resolve(false); };
        const onForce = () => { cleanup(); resolve(true); };

        btnCancel.addEventListener('click', onCancel);
        btnForce.addEventListener('click', onForce);
    });
}

// --- FONCTIONS MODALE DÉTAILS KPI (Présents / Hors Prod / Absences) ---

let currentKpiModalData = []; // On stocke maintenant des objets {name, status}

function openKpiDetailsModal(kpiType) {
    if (!state.indicatorData) return;

    let itemsList = [];
    let title = "";
    let icon = "";
    let colorClass = "";

    const dailyCompagnons = state.indicatorData.compagnons.daily;
    const dailyInterimaires = state.indicatorData.interimaires.daily;

    // Fonction pour extraire les noms ET les statuts
    const extractData = (keysArray) => {
        keysArray.forEach(k => {
            (dailyCompagnons[k] || []).forEach(name => itemsList.push({ name: name, status: k }));
            (dailyInterimaires[k] || []).forEach(name => itemsList.push({ name: name, status: k }));
        });
    };

    // RÈGLES STRICTES DE CATÉGORISATION
    if (kpiType === 'presence') {
        title = t('kpi_present_day') ? t('kpi_present_day').replace(/ \(.+\)/,'') : 'Présents';
        icon = "fa-users";
        colorClass = "bg-[#00205b]";
        extractData(['presence']); // Présents purs
        
    } else if (kpiType === 'hors_prod') {
        title = t('kpi_out_of_prod') || 'Hors Prod.';
        icon = "fa-user-clock";
        colorClass = "bg-purple-500";
        extractData(['S', 'Ecole', 'P', 'Z', 'F', '4HF', 'Mi', 'D']);
        
    } else if (kpiType === 'absences') {
        title = t('kpi_absences_day') ? t('kpi_absences_day').replace(/ \(.+\)/,'') : 'Absences';
        icon = "fa-user-slash";
        colorClass = "bg-rose-500";
        extractData(['CET', 'CP', '4HCP', 'JRTT', 'Abs', 'RF', 'Ma', 'LMa']);
    }

    // On dédoublonne (au cas où) et on trie par ordre alphabétique (A-Z)
    const uniqueMap = new Map();
    itemsList.forEach(item => {
        if (!uniqueMap.has(item.name)) uniqueMap.set(item.name, item);
    });
    currentKpiModalData = Array.from(uniqueMap.values()).sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name));

    // Mise à jour du visuel de la modale
    document.getElementById('kpi-modal-title').textContent = title;
    document.getElementById('kpi-modal-count').textContent = currentKpiModalData.length;
    
    const iconContainer = document.getElementById('kpi-modal-icon-container');
    iconContainer.className = `w-12 h-12 rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center text-white shadow-lg rotate-3 ${colorClass}`;
    document.getElementById('kpi-modal-icon').className = `fas ${icon} text-xl`;
    
    document.getElementById('kpi-modal-search').value = '';
    
    renderKpiModalList();
    document.getElementById('kpi-details-modal').classList.remove('hidden');
}

function renderKpiModalList() {
    const ul = document.getElementById('kpi-modal-list');
    if (!ul) return;
    
    if (currentKpiModalData.length === 0) {
        ul.innerHTML = `<li class="text-center p-6 text-gray-400 font-bold text-xs uppercase tracking-widest border border-dashed border-gray-200 rounded-xl bg-white/50">${t('modal_empty_list') || 'Aucune personne dans cette catégorie.'}</li>`;
        return;
    }

    ul.innerHTML = currentKpiModalData.map(item => {
        let statusBadge = '';
        
        // Si c'est autre chose qu'une simple "présence", on affiche le motif
        if (item.status && item.status !== 'presence') {
            // Attribution des couleurs des badges selon la gravité/type
            let badgeColor = 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-600 border-gray-200';
            if (['Ma', 'LMa', 'Abs', 'RF', 'D'].includes(item.status)) badgeColor = 'bg-rose-50 text-rose-600 border-rose-100';
            else if (['CP', '4HCP', 'JRTT', 'CET'].includes(item.status)) badgeColor = 'bg-emerald-50 text-emerald-600 border-emerald-100';
            else if (['Mi', 'F', '4HF', 'Ecole', 'P', 'S', 'Z'].includes(item.status)) badgeColor = 'bg-purple-50 text-purple-600 border-purple-100';

            // On récupère le vrai nom du statut (traduit ou depuis la base)
            const translatedKey = 'status_' + item.status;
            const label = (t(translatedKey) !== translatedKey) ? t(translatedKey) : (STATUSES[item.status] || item.status);
            
            statusBadge = `<span class="px-2.5 py-1.5 rounded-lg text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest ${badgeColor} shadow-sm border shrink-0 truncate max-w-[120px] text-center">${label}</span>`;
        }

        return `
        <li class="kpi-list-item flex justify-between items-center bg-white/80 backdrop-blur-sm p-4 rounded-2xl border border-white shadow-sm hover:shadow-md hover:bg-white transition-all mb-3 group">
            <div class="flex items-center gap-3 min-w-0 pr-2">
                <div class="w-8 h-8 rounded-xl bg-[#00205b]/5 text-[#00b5e2] flex items-center justify-center group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform shrink-0">
                    <i class="fas fa-user text-sm"></i>
                </div>
                <span class="text-[11px] sm:text-xs font-black text-[#00205b] uppercase tracking-widest truncate kpi-name-target">${item.name}</span>
            </div>
            ${statusBadge}
        </li>`;
    }).join('');
}

function filterKpiModalList() {
    const query = document.getElementById('kpi-modal-search').value.toLowerCase().trim();
    const items = document.querySelectorAll('#kpi-modal-list .kpi-list-item');
    
    items.forEach(item => {
        const name = item.querySelector('.kpi-name-target').textContent.toLowerCase();
        if (name.includes(query)) {
            item.style.display = '';
        } else {
            item.style.display = 'none';
        }
    });
}

function closeKpiDetailsModal() {
    document.getElementById('kpi-details-modal').classList.add('hidden');
}

// Ferme la fenêtre si on clique en dehors
document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
    const modal = document.getElementById('kpi-details-modal');
    if (modal && !modal.classList.contains('hidden')) {
        if (e.target === modal) {
            closeKpiDetailsModal();
        }
    }
});

// Ouvre ou ferme la grande fenêtre d'aide
function toggleChatbot() {
  const chatWindow = document.getElementById('chat-window');
  const isHidden = chatWindow.classList.contains('hidden');
  
  if (isHidden) {
    // ON OUVRE : On force le rendu des catégories pour prendre la bonne langue
    renderHelpCategories();
    chatWindow.classList.remove('hidden');
  } else {
    // ON FERME
    chatWindow.classList.add('hidden');
  }
}

// Affiche la GRILLE des catégories principales dans la bonne langue
function renderHelpCategories() {
  document.getElementById('help-breadcrumbs').classList.add('hidden');
  const container = document.getElementById('help-content-area');
  
  // Récupère la langue active
  const currentLang = localStorage.getItem('app_language') || 'fr';
  const db = helpDatabase[currentLang] || helpDatabase['fr'];
  
  let html = `
    <div class="text-center mb-4 mt-2 fade-in-panel">
        <h3 class="text-[#00205b] font-black text-xl tracking-tight">${t('help_ask')}</h3>
        <p class="text-gray-400 text-xs font-bold mt-1">${t('help_select')}</p>
    </div>
    <div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4 fade-in-panel pb-4">
  `;
  
  for (const key in db) {
    const cat = db[key];
    html += `
      <div onclick="selectHelpCategory('${key}')" class="flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-6 bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-[2rem] shadow-sm hover:shadow-[0_15px_30px_rgba(0,181,226,0.15)] hover:border-[#00b5e2]/40 transition-all cursor-pointer group transform hover:-translate-y-1">
        <div class="w-16 h-16 rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center text-3xl shadow-inner mb-4 ${cat.color} group-hover:scale-110 group-hover:bg-[#00b5e2] group-hover:text-white transition-all duration-300">
          <i class="fas ${cat.icon}"></i>
        </div>
        <span class="text-[11px] font-black text-[#00205b] text-center uppercase tracking-widest leading-tight group-hover:text-[#00b5e2] transition-colors">${cat.title}</span>
      </div>
    `;
  }
  
  html += `</div>`;
  container.innerHTML = html;
}

// Affiche l'écran des questions pour une catégorie
function selectHelpCategory(key) {
  const currentLang = localStorage.getItem('app_language') || 'fr';
  const db = helpDatabase[currentLang] || helpDatabase['fr'];
  const cat = db[key];
  if (!cat) return;
  
  document.getElementById('current-category-title').textContent = cat.title;
  document.getElementById('help-breadcrumbs').classList.remove('hidden');
  
  const container = document.getElementById('help-content-area');
  
  let html = `<div class="flex flex-col gap-3 fade-in-panel">`;
  
  cat.questions.forEach((item, index) => {
    html += `
      <div class="faq-item border-2 border-transparent bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm hover:shadow-md hover:border-[#00b5e2]/20 transition-all overflow-hidden" id="faq-${key}-${index}">
        <div onclick="toggleFaqAccordion('${key}-${index}')" class="p-5 flex items-center justify-between gap-4 cursor-pointer select-none group">
          <div class="flex gap-4 items-center">
            <i class="fas fa-question-circle text-[#00b5e2] text-xl opacity-50 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity"></i>
            <span class="text-xs font-black text-[#00205b] uppercase tracking-wide leading-snug">${item.q}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-gray-50 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 group-hover:bg-[#00b5e2]/10 faq-chevron transition-all duration-300">
            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down text-gray-400"></i>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="faq-answer px-6 border-t border-gray-50 text-slate-600 text-[13px] font-medium leading-relaxed bg-slate-50/50">
          ${item.a}
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
  });
  
  html += `</div>`;
  container.innerHTML = html;
}

function toggleFaqAccordion(id) {
  const target = document.getElementById('faq-' + id);
  if (!target) return;
  const isActive = target.classList.contains('active');
  
  document.querySelectorAll('.faq-item').forEach(item => {
    item.classList.remove('active');
  });
  
  if (!isActive) target.classList.add('active');
}

function goBackToCategories() {
  renderHelpCategories();
}

// ÉCOUTEUR GLOBAL
document.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
    const chatWindow = document.getElementById('chat-window');
    const fabButton = document.getElementById('chatbot-fab');
    
    if (chatWindow && !chatWindow.classList.contains('hidden')) {
        const path = event.composedPath();
        if (!path.includes(chatWindow) && !path.includes(fabButton)) {
            toggleChatbot();
        }
    }
});

function toggleChatbot() {
  const chatWindow = document.getElementById('chat-window');
  chatWindow.classList.toggle('hidden');
  if (chatWindow.classList.contains('hidden')) {
    setTimeout(() => { renderHelpCategories(); }, 400);
  }
}

// ============================================================
// ÉCOUTEUR GLOBAL : BUG DU CLIC CORRIGÉ !
// ============================================================
document.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
    const chatWindow = document.getElementById('chat-window');
    const fabButton = document.getElementById('chatbot-fab');
    
    if (chatWindow && !chatWindow.classList.contains('hidden')) {
        // composedPath() permet de retracer l'origine du clic MÊME SI l'élément a été détruit par le JS
        const path = event.composedPath();
        
        // Si le chemin du clic ne contient ni la fenêtre de chat, ni le bouton = on a cliqué en dehors
        if (!path.includes(chatWindow) && !path.includes(fabButton)) {
            toggleChatbot();
        }
    }
});

let trendChartInstance = null;

function renderTrendChartModern(labels, dataValues) {
    const ctx = document.getElementById('trend-chart-modern');
    if(!ctx) return;
    
    const context = ctx.getContext('2d');
    
    const gradient = context.createLinearGradient(0, 0, 0, 400);
    gradient.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(244, 63, 94, 0.4)'); 
    gradient.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0)');

    if (trendChartInstance) trendChartInstance.destroy();

    // 🔴 MAGIE DE TRADUCTION : On récupère les mots du dictionnaire
    // On prend "Présents (Jour)" et on coupe le "(Jour)"
    const labelPresent = t('kpi_present_day') ? t('kpi_present_day').replace(/ \(.+\)/,'') : 'Présents';
    // On récupère "collaborateur(s)"
    const labelCollab = t('modal_detail_collab') || 'collaborateurs';

    trendChartInstance = new Chart(context, {
        type: 'line',
        data: {
            labels: labels,
            datasets: [{
                label: labelPresent, // Appliqué ici
                data: dataValues,
                borderColor: '#f43f5e',
                borderWidth: 3,
                pointBackgroundColor: '#ffffff',
                pointBorderColor: '#f43f5e',
                pointBorderWidth: 2,
                pointRadius: 0, 
                pointHoverRadius: 6,
                pointHitRadius: 20, 
                fill: true,
                backgroundColor: gradient,
                tension: 0.4 
            }]
        },
        options: {
            responsive: true,
            maintainAspectRatio: false,
            interaction: {
                mode: 'index',
                intersect: false,
            },
            plugins: {
                legend: { display: false },
                datalabels: { display: false },
                tooltip: {
                    enabled: true,
                    backgroundColor: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.95)',
                    titleColor: '#00205b',
                    titleFont: { size: 13, weight: '900', family: "'Inter', sans-serif" },
                    bodyColor: '#f43f5e',
                    bodyFont: { size: 14, weight: 'bold', family: "'Inter', sans-serif" },
                    borderColor: '#e2e8f0',
                    borderWidth: 1,
                    padding: 12,
                    boxPadding: 6,
                    cornerRadius: 12,
                    displayColors: false,
                    callbacks: {
                        label: function(context) {
                            // 🔴 TRADUCTION : On affiche "X collaborateur(s)"
                            return context.parsed.y + ' ' + labelCollab;
                        }
                    },
                    boxShadow: '0 10px 25px -5px rgba(0, 32, 91, 0.1)'
                }
            },
            scales: {
                x: { 
                    grid: { display: false },
                    ticks: { color: '#94a3b8', font: { weight: 'bold', size: 10 } }
                },
                y: {
                    beginAtZero: true,
                    grid: { color: '#f1f5f9', borderDash: [5, 5] },
                    ticks: { color: '#94a3b8', font: { weight: 'bold' } }
                }
            }
        }
    });
}

</script>
